namespace = MYTH_WoL
# Mythos - Way of Life events

# MYTH_WoL.1 - Summon Familiar - was MYTH.94
character_event = {
	id = "MYTH_WoL.1"
	title = "EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.1"
	desc = "EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.1"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunting_scene
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		# This event requires magic
		OR = {
			trait = novice_mage
			trait = eldritch_scholar
			trait = veteran_wizard
			trait = arcane_master
		}
		NOR = { 
			has_character_modifier = cat_familiar
			has_character_modifier = wolf_familiar
			has_character_modifier = owl_familiar
			has_character_modifier = raven_familiar
			has_character_modifier = dove_familiar
		}
		OR = {
			stewardship = 8
			martial = 8
			diplomacy = 8
			intrigue = 8
			learning = 8
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { months = 72 }
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = eldritch_scholar
				trait = veteran_wizard
				trait = arcane_master
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = { 
				has_character_modifier = cat_familiar
				has_character_modifier = wolf_familiar
				has_character_modifier = owl_familiar
				has_character_modifier = raven_familiar
				has_character_modifier = dove_familiar
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Dove
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.1
		trigger = { 
			diplomacy = 8
			NOT = { trait = wroth }
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -50 }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.2 days = 150 }
					set_character_flag = summoning_familiar_dove
				}
				10 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.3 days = 150 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { ai_ambition = 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ai_honor = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = cruel
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Wolf
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.1
		trigger = { martial = 8 }
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -50 }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = {
				90 = { 
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.2 days = 150 }
					set_character_flag = summoning_familiar_wolf
				}
				10 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.3 days = 150 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = werewolf
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = vampire
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				ai_ambition = 30
				independent = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = adventurer
					trait = peasant_leader
					trait = varangian
					trait = viking
					trait = ravager
					trait = seaking
					trait = shieldmaiden
					trait = sea_queen
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Crow
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.1
		trigger = { stewardship = 8 }
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -50 }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = {
				90 = { 
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.2 days = 150 }
					set_character_flag = summoning_familiar_crow
				}
				10 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.3 days = 150 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_character_flag = god_odin
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = dragon
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = deceitful
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Rat
		name = EVTOPTD_MYTH_WoL.1
		trigger = { intrigue = 8 }
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -50 }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = {
				90 = { 
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.2 days = 150 }
					set_character_flag = summoning_familiar_rat
				}
				10 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.3 days = 150 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = has_bubonic_plague
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = bastard
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = paranoid
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_any_kinslayer_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Owl
		name = EVTOPTE_MYTH_WoL.1
		trigger = { learning = 8 }
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -50 }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			random_list = {
				90 = { 
					character_event = {
						id = MYTH_WoL.2
						days = 150
					}
					set_character_flag = summoning_familiar_owl
				}
				10 = {
					character_event = { 
						id = MYTH_WoL.3
						days = 150
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_character_flag = god_athena
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = erudite
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					trait = scholar
					trait = faqih
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = pilgrim
					trait = hajjaj
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = nun
					trait = monk
					trait = hafiz
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = heresiarch
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Opt out
		name = EVTOPTF_MYTH_WoL.1
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.2 }
				ai = no
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.2 - was MYTH.95 - Summon Familiar event success
character_event = {
	id = "MYTH_WoL.2"
	title = "EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.2"
	desc = "EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.2"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunting_scene
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 2 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.2
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = summoning_familiar_dove
		}
		prestige = 10
		add_character_modifier = { name = dove_familiar duration = -1 }
		clr_character_flag = summoning_familiar_dove
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.2
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = summoning_familiar_wolf
		}
		prestige = 10
		add_character_modifier = { name = wolf_familiar duration = -1 }
		clr_character_flag = summoning_familiar_wolf
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.2
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = summoning_familiar_crow
		}
		prestige = 10
		add_character_modifier = { name = raven_familiar duration = -1 }
		clr_character_flag = summoning_familiar_crow
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.2
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = summoning_familiar_owl
		}
		prestige = 10
		add_character_modifier = { name = owl_familiar duration = -1 }
		clr_character_flag = summoning_familiar_owl
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.2
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = summoning_familiar_rat
		}
		prestige = 10
		add_character_modifier = { name = cat_familiar duration = -1 }
		clr_character_flag = summoning_familiar_rat
	}
}

			FROM = { trait = novice_mage }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = "EVTDESCB_MYTH_WoL.5"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { trait = eldritch_scholar }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = "EVTDESCC_MYTH_WoL.5"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { trait = veteran_wizard }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = "EVTDESCD_MYTH_WoL.5"

			FROM = { trait = arcane_master }
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.5"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { trait = novice_mage }
		}
		tooltip = { FROM = { add_trait = novice_mage } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.5"
		trigger = {
			FROM = { trait = eldritch_scholar }
		}
		tooltip = { FROM = { add_trait = eldritch_scholar } }

		name = "EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.5"

		name = "EXCELLENT"

		}
		tooltip = { FROM = { add_trait = arcane_master } }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.6 - was MYTH.109 - You've been uncovered as a werewolf - snitched
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.6
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.6
	desc = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.6
	
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.6
		trigger = {
			NOT = { culture = werewolf_culture }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.6
		trigger = {
			culture = werewolf_culture
		}
	}
	after = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = exposed_me
		}
		add_trait = known_werewolf
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = known_monster
			remove_trait = secret_werewolf
		}
	}
}

	
# MYTH_WoL.7 - was MYTH.110 - Someone in your court is a werewolf - informed
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.7
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.7
	desc = { # Not werewolf or werewolf culture - they are a monster
		text = EVTDESCA_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = werewolf }
			NOT = { culture = werewolf_culture }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Werewolf culture looks up to werewolves
		text = EVTDESCB_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = werewolf }
			culture = werewolf_culture
		}
	}
	desc = { # Hidden werewolf needs to keep their cover
		text = EVTDESCC_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			trait = werewolf
			NOT = { trait = known_werewolf }
		}
	}
	desc = { # Another known werewolf
		text = EVTDESCD_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			trait = known_werewolf
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_evt_eavesdropping
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		#NOT = { trait = incapable }
	}
	
	# Most people just hate you
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.7	
		trigger = {
			NOT = { trait = werewolf }
			NOT = { culture = werewolf_culture }
		}
		
		opinion = {
			modifier = newly_found_werewolf
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_MYTH_WoL.7 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = monster_hunter
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	# Secret werewolves can take advantage of this
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			trait = werewolf
			NOT = { trait = known_werewolf }
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = newly_found_werewolf
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_MYTH_WoL.7}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = monster_hunter
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
	# Werewolf culture views this positively - impressed toward werewolf, approves of my behavior from werewolf
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = { culture = werewolf_culture }
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_approves
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = approves_of_my_behaviour
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	# Werewolf culture + ambitious is envious. May gain envious trait
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			culture = werewolf_culture
			OR = {
				trait = ambitious
				trait = envious
			}
			NOT = { trait = werewolf }
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_envy
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_trait = envious
			hidden_tooltip = {
				# Notify
				character_event = { id = 38271 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				opinion = { who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf value = 50 }
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf value = 50 } }
				factor = 0.8
			}
		}
	}
	# Werewolves can ignore it
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTE_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = { trait = werewolf }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	# Werewolves can also choose to reveal themselves. Gain temporary bonuses.
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTF_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {
			trait = werewolf
			NOT = { trait = known_werewolf }
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = deliberate_reveal_werewolf
			duration = 360
		}
		add_trait = known_werewolf
		increase_control = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = known_monster
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.14 days = 1 } }
			any_realm_character = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.15 days = 1 } } # Court finds out character is a werewolf
			liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.15 days = 1} } # Liege finds out character is a werewolf
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPF_MYTH_WoL.7 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = { martial = 10 }
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					trait = strong
					trait = robust
				}
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = impaler
				factor = 1.2
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = wroth
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = brave
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = craven
				factor = 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = deceitful
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = berserker
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}	
	# Known werewolves approve
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTG_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = {	trait = known_werewolf }
		opinion = {
			modifier = likes_newly_found_werewolf
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 150
		}
	}		
	# Known werewolves can try to become friends
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTH_MYTH_WoL.7
		trigger = { 
			trait = known_werewolf
			NOR = {
				is_friend = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
				trait = shy
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = likes_newly_found_werewolf
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.16 days = 3 random = 3 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				trait = gregarious
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = shy
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = trusting
				factor = 1.2
			}
			modifier = {
				trait = paranoid
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH.56 }
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.8 - was MYTH.111 - Your vassal/courtier is a werewolf - informed
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.8
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.8
	picture = GFX_evt_eavesdropping
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Human announcement
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = werewolf
				culture = werewolf_culture
			}
		}
	}
	# Werewolf Culture announcement
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			culture = werewolf_culture
			NOT = { trait = werewolf }
		}
	}
	# Secret werewolf announcement
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCC_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			trait = werewolf
			NOT = { trait = known_werewolf }
		}
	}
	# Known Werewolf announcement
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCD_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			trait = known_werewolf
		}
	}
	
	# Arrest him with silver weapons (Non-werewolf) 
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.8
		tooltip_info = martial
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = known_werewolf
				culture = werewolf_culture
			}
			martial = 12
		}
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.3 min = 50 max = 200 }
		event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = {
			imprison = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}
	}
	# Let go for favor
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTE_MYTH_WoL.8
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = known_werewolf
				culture = werewolf_culture
			}
			intrigue = 12
			has_dlc = "Zeus" # For favors
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.19 days = 1 } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPE_MYTH_WoL.8 }
	}
	# He gets one last chance (Non-werewolf)
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = werewolf
				culture = werewolf_culture
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = newly_found_werewolf
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			years = 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
	}
	# Pleased (Werewolf culture or known werewolf)
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = werewolf_culture
				trait = known_werewolf
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_pleased
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			months = 6
		}
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_pleased
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			months = 6
		}
	}
	# No concern of mine (Werewolf or werewolf culture)
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_MYTH_WoL.8
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture = werewolf_culture
				trait = werewolf
			}
		}
	}
}

	
# MYTH_WoL.9 - was MYTH.112 - Werewolf discovered
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.9
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.9
	desc = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.9
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		# Expose the werewolf
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.9
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_liege_of = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
				AND = {
					trait = monster_hunter
					event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = {
						at_location = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = monster_hunter
				trait = vampire
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = werewolf
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf value = 0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = { who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf value = 50 }
			}
		}
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			modifier = exposed_me
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_MYTH_WoL.9 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.6 } } # Character uncovered as a werewolf
			any_realm_character = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.7 } } # Court finds out character is a werewolf
			if = {
				limit = {
					independent = no
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.8 } } # Liege finds out character is a werewolf
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		# Inform Liege
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.9
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_liege_of = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf }
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { independent = no }
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { liege = { NOT = { war_with = ROOT } } }
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { liege = { NOT = { trait = known_werewolf } } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				trait = monster_hunter
			}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPB_MYTH_WoL.9 }
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.10 } } }
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		# Blackmail to prevent factionalism
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.9
		trigger = {
			is_liege_of = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = {
				is_playable = yes
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = liege modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 10.0
				event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = {
					in_faction = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = werewolf
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.6
				trait = monster_hunter
			}
		}
			
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPC_MYTH_WoL.9 }
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			modifier = opinion_spy_blackmailed
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.12 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		# Blackmail to join faction
		name = EVTOPTD_MYTH_WoL.9
		trigger = {
			same_liege = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = {
				ai = yes
				is_playable = yes
				NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_coerced_into_joining_faction } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 110
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				trait = monster_hunter
			}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPD_MYTH_WoL.9 }
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = event_target:target_discovered_werewolf
			modifier = opinion_spy_blackmailed
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:target_discovered_werewolf = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.11 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		# Keep it to yourself
		name = EVTOPTE_MYTH_WoL.9
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 90
				trait = werewolf
			}
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPE_MYTH_WoL.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTF_MYTH_WoL.9
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPF_MYTH_WoL.9 }
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = WoL.2069 }
		}
	}
}

### Studying in Scholomance
# MYTH_WoL.20 - was MYTHMORE.19 - Invited to Scholomance
character_event = {
	id = "MYTH_WoL.20"
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.20
	desc = "EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.20"
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_scholarship
		NOT = { religion = the_damned }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.20
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = novice_mage
					trait = deceitful
					religion = satanist
					trait = vampire
				}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = study_at_scholomance
			duration = -1
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						trait = novice_mage
						trait = eldritch_scholar
						trait = veteran_wizard
						trait = arcane_master
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.21 days = 180 }
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							religion = messalian
							religion = satanist
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.22 days = 180 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						religion = messalian
					}
					character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.27 days = 180 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit =  { religion = satanist }
					if = {
						limit = {
							trait = novice_mage
						}
						character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.29 days = 180 }
						break = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { trait = vampire }
						}
						character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.30 days = 180 }
						break = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							trait = eldritch_scholar
						}
						character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.31 days = 180 }
						break = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
						}
						character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.32 days = 180 }
						break = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.20
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = WoL.6329 days = 180 } }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.21 - was MYTHMORE.20 - Learning elementry magic at Scholomance
character_event = {
	id = "MYTH_WoL.21"
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.21
	desc = "EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.21"
	picture = GFX_evt_relaxed_ruler
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_scholarship
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.21
		add_trait = novice_mage
		update_natural_magic = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = magic_heritage } }
			add_trait = magic_heritage
		}
		remove_trait = amateurish_plotter
		remove_trait = flamboyant_schemer
		remove_trait = intricate_webweaver
		remove_trait = elusive_shadow
		remove_trait = naive_appeaser
		remove_trait = underhanded_rogue
		remove_trait = charismatic_negotiator
		remove_trait = grey_eminence
		remove_trait = indulgent_wastrel
		remove_trait = thrifty_clerk
		remove_trait = fortune_builder
		remove_trait = midas_touched
		remove_trait = misguided_warrior
		remove_trait = tough_soldier
		remove_trait = skilled_tactician
		remove_trait = brilliant_strategist
		remove_trait = detached_priest
		remove_trait = martial_cleric
		remove_trait = scholarly_theologian
		remove_trait = mastermind_theologian
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = amateurish_plotter
					trait = naive_appeaser
					trait = indulgent_wastrel
					trait = misguided_warrior
					trait = detached_priest
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = erudite
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						religion = messalian
						religion = satanist
						religion = yazidi
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.22 days = 180 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					religion = yazidi
				}
				character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.27 days = 180 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					religion = messalian
				}
				character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.27 days = 180 }
			}
			else = { # Satanist
				if = {
					limit = {
						trait = novice_mage
					}
					character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.29 days = 180 }
					break = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { trait = vampire }
					}
					character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.30 days = 180 }
					break = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						trait = eldritch_scholar
					}
					character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.31 days = 180 }
					break = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
					}
					character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.32 days = 180 }
					break = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.21
		remove_character_modifier = study_at_scholomance
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = WoL.6329 days = 180 } }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.22 - was MYTHMORE.21 - Religious authorities find out about Scholomance
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.22
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_scholarship
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_head = { is_alive = yes }
				religion_head = { ai = yes }
				# Don't need to check Religion - already skipped for Satanist and Messalian
			}
			religion_head = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.23 } # Religious head opines
			}
			break = yes
		}
		character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.27 } # Else skip to next
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.24 - MYTHMORE.23 - Scholomance -  A letter from religious head - respond
letter_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.24
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.24
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_MYTH_WoL.24
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion_group = christian # Messalians should never get to this event
				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = jewish_group
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_MYTH_WoL.24
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				religion_group = christian # Messalians should never get to this event
				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = jewish_group
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.24 # Tell them to get lost
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = cynical
					trait = scholar
					trait = mystic
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = excommunicated
				trait = decadent
			}
		}
		piety = -100
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = brave } }
			add_trait = brave
		}
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_branded_heretic
			who = FROM
			years = 10
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = annoyed_religious
			years = 2
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			# Religious head will try to excommunicate
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.25 days = 10 }
			}
			# Continue with event chain
			character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.27 days = 180 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.24 # Abandon Scholomance
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 40
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = pilgrim
					trait = monk
					trait = nun
					trait = hajjaj
					trait = hafiz
					trait = crusader
					trait = mujahid
					trait = shaddai
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_pleased
			who = FROM
			years = 3
		}
		opinion = {
			modifier = saved_my_soul
			who = FROM
			years = 3
		}
		remove_character_modifier = study_at_scholomance
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = WoL.6329 days = 180 } }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH.56 }
		}
	}
}

			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
				}
				character_event = { id=MYTH_WoL.32 days = 180 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.28
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
				trait = theologian
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					trait = pilgrim
					trait = monk
					trait = nun
					trait = hajjaj
					trait = hafiz
					trait = saoshyant
					trait = crusader
					trait = mujahid
					trait = valhalla_bound
					trait = eagle_warrior
					trait = sun_warrior
					trait = ukkos_shield
					trait = nyames_shield
					trait = peruns_chosen
					trait = romuvas_own
					trait = ares_own
					trait = tengri_warrior
					trait = shaddai
					trait = gondi_shahansha
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					true_religion_group = christian
					true_religion_group = muslim
					true_religion_group = jewish_group
				}
				NOT = { 
					true_religion = messalian
					true_religion = yazidi
				}
			}
		}
		remove_character_modifier = study_at_scholomance
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = WoL.6329 days = 180 } }
	}
	
	after = {

		}

### Becoming a werewolf during a hunt
# MYTH_WoL.33 - was MYTHMORE.32 - Bit by a possible werewolf
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.33
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.33
	
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.33
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			trait = werewolf 
			trait = dragon
			trait = demon_trait
			trait = ethereal_trait
			trait = vampire
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.33
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = NONE
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 33
					trait = rabies
					trait = possessed
					flag = checked_race
				}
				new_character = {
					imprison = ROOT
					add_trait = werewolf
					add_trait = secret_werewolf
					#character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.35 days = 40 random = 40 }
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = { id = MYTH.56 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_rabies }
					}
					give_rabies_effect = yes
					set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 40 random = 40 }
				}
			}
			20 = {
				create_character = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = NONE
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
					female = no
					age = 33
					trait = rabies
					trait = possessed
					flag = checked_race
				}
				new_character = {
					imprison = ROOT
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = { id = MYTH.56 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_rabies }
					}
					give_rabies_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.33
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_rabies }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_dlc = "Reapers"
							}
						}
						add_trait = ill
						hidden_tooltip = { 
							set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_trait = fever
						hidden_tooltip = {
							set_character_flag = got_rabies
							set_character_flag = developing_illness
							set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
							character_event = { id = RIP.5024 days = 14 random = 14 }
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			20 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_rabies }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_dlc = "Reapers"
							}
						}
						add_trait = ill
					}
					else = {
						add_trait = fever
						set_character_flag = got_rabies
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5024 days = 14 random = 14 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.34 - was MYTHMORE.33 - Rabies develops into werewolf
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.34
	title = "EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.34"
	desc = "EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.34"
	picture = GFX_evt_wolf
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	capable_only = yes
	min_age = 18
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trait = rabies
			trait = ill
		}
		has_character_flag = werewolf_bite
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPT_MYTH_WoL.34"
		add_trait = werewolf
		add_trait = secret_werewolf
		set_variable = { which = control value = 1 }
		add_trait = control_1
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_trait = rabies
			remove_trait = ill
			remove_trait = fever
			remove_trait = fatigue
			remove_trait = malaise
			# Just in case they also have a second illness...
			remove_trait = cough
			remove_trait = diarrhea
			remove_trait = vomiting
			remove_trait = chest_pain
			remove_trait = cramps
			remove_trait = rash
			remove_trait = headache
			remove_trait = abdominal_pain
			remove_trait = infection
			clr_character_flag = werewolf_bite
			clr_character_flag = developing_illness
			clr_character_flag = got_rabies
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.36 - was MYTHMORE.35 - Stewardship event - suspected werewolf peasant
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.36
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.36
	desc = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.36
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_economy
	
	min_age = 16
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	capable_only = yes
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_rulership
		NOT = { has_character_flag = in_seclusion }
		NOT = { culture = werewolf_culture }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = secret_werewolf
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		# Hunt down and kill
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.36
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -75 }
		random_demesne_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wild_wolfman_killed
				duration = 180
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_wounded_effect = yes
		}
		random = {
			chance = 1
			death = { death_reason = death_werewolf }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 20
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_rabies }
					NOR = {
						race_disease_resist = yes
						race_disease_immune = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dlc = "Reapers"
						}
					}
					add_trait = ill
					hidden_tooltip = { 
						set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
						character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_trait = fever
					hidden_tooltip = {
						set_character_flag = got_rabies
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
						character_event = { id = RIP.5024 days = 14 random = 14 }
						character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_character = {
				if = {
					limit = { trait = werewolf }
					opinion = { modifier = opinion_unhappy who = ROOT months = 24 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Hunt down and arrest
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.36
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.1 min = -2 max = -40 }
		random_demesne_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wild_wolfman_arrested
				duration = 180
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 10
			add_wounded_effect = yes
		}
		random = {
			chance = 10
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = immune_rabies }
					NOR = {
						race_disease_resist = yes
						race_disease_immune = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dlc = "Reapers"
						}
					}
					add_trait = ill
					hidden_tooltip = { 
						set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
						character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_trait = fever
					hidden_tooltip = {
						set_character_flag = got_rabies
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						set_character_flag = werewolf_bite
						character_event = { id = RIP.5024 days = 14 random = 14 }
						character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.34 days = 60 random = 60 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_character = {
				if = {
					limit = { trait = werewolf }
					opinion = { modifier = opinion_unhappy who = ROOT months = 24 }
				}
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = NONE
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			age = 33
			trait = possessed
			flag = checked_race
		}
		new_character = {
			imprison = ROOT
			random = {
				chance = 70
				add_trait = werewolf
				add_trait = known_werewolf
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.36
		random_demesne_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wild_wolfman_ignored
				duration = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.37 - was MYTHMORE.36 - Stewardship event - wild child found. Peasants think he is a werewolf
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.37
	title = EVTNAME_MYTH_WoL.37
	desc = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL.37
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_economy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	only_playable = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_rulership
		NOT = { has_character_flag = in_seclusion }
		NOT = { trait = dragon }
		NOT = { trait = zombie }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = {
				any_child = {
					is_female = no
					count = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_ambition = obj_have_a_son
				has_ambition = obj_groom_an_heir
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = NONE
			religion = ROOT
			culture = ROOT
			female = no
			age = 7
			trait = rowdy
			trait = pup
			flag = checked_race
		}
		new_character = {
			set_variable = { which = control value = 4 }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				new_character = { add_trait = brooding }
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Kill the child
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.37
		new_character = {
			death = {
				death_reason = death_execution
				killer = ROOT
			}
		}
		random_demesne_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wild_wolfman_killed
				duration = 180
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 33
			add_trait = cruel
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_character = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = killed_child
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_MYTH_WoL.37 }
	}
	# Send the child back to the woods
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.37
		new_character = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				save_event_target_as = new_court
			}
			move_character = event_target:new_court
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.38 days = 10 random = 5 }
		}
		random_demesne_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = wild_wolfman_ignored
				duration = 180
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_character = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = abandoned_child
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPB_MYTH_WoL.37 }
	}
	# Take care of the child yourself
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.37
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_ward = { count = 2 }
			}
		}
		new_character = {
			set_guardian = ROOT
		}
	}
	# Adopt the child as your own
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_MYTH_WoL.37
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_child = {
					is_female = no
					count = 1
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_ambition = obj_have_a_son
				has_ambition = obj_groom_an_heir
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_married = yes }
			spouse = { save_event_target_as = event_spouse }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }
			new_character = {
				set_mother = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = yes }
				new_character = {
					set_father = event_target:event_spouse
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			#limit = { is_female = no }
			new_character = {
				set_father = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_married = yes }
				new_character = {
					set_mother = event_target:event_spouse
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH.56 }
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.38

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	ai = yes
	max_age = 16

# MYTH_WoL.39 - Choose magic specialization
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.39
	title = EVTNAMEMYTH_WoL.39
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.39
	picture = GFX_evt_comet
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		NOR = {
			has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
			has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
			has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
			has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		}
		NOR = {
			trait = summoner
			trait = enchanter
			trait = alchemist
			trait = herbalist
			trait = necromancer
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
				has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
				has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
				has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
				has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { has_focus = focus_magic }
		}
	}
	
	# Study conjuration - Requires magic
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.39
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = eldritch_scholar
				trait = veteran_wizard
				trait = arcane_master
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ai_ambition = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { ai_rationality = 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				martial = 12
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { max_manpower = 1000 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				war = yes
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = { name = studying_conjuration duration = -1 }
	}
	# Study sorcery - Requires magic
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.39
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = eldritch_scholar
				trait = veteran_wizard
				trait = arcane_master
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { diplomacy = 9 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				intrigue = 12
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_polygamy = yes
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = { name = studying_sorcery duration = -1 }
	}
	# Study alchemy - does not require magic
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.39
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ai_greed = 30
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ai_greed = 60
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				wealth = 200
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = { name = studying_alchemy duration = -1 }
	}
	# Study herbalism - does not require magic
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.39
		# Hide this into a second menu if you have magic and can study necromancy directly
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NAND = {
					OR = {
						trait = novice_mage
						trait = eldritch_scholar
						trait = veteran_wizard
						trait = arcane_master
					}
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = allow_necromancy_study
					}
				}
				ai = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_ill = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				any_child = { is_ill = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				any_lover = { is_ill = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				any_spouse = { is_ill = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { health = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = { name = studying_herbalism duration = -1 }
	}
	
	# Second page of options if necromancy is available
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					trait = novice_mage
					trait = eldritch_scholar
					trait = veteran_wizard
					trait = arcane_master
				}
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_bloodline_flag = allow_necromancy_study
				}
				ai = no
			}
		}
		name = EVTOPTEMYTH_WoL.39
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.298 }
	}
	
	# Necromancy for AI
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.39
		# Only visible to AI, they don't use the second page
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					trait = novice_mage
					trait = eldritch_scholar
					trait = veteran_wizard
					trait = arcane_master
				}
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_bloodline_flag = allow_necromancy_study
				}
				ai = yes
			}
		}

# MYTH_WoL.40 - Magic Level Up
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.40
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
			has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
			has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
			has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		}
		has_focus = focus_magic
	}

	immediate = {
		# Select random effect
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					OR = {
						trait = arcane_master
						NOR = {
							trait = novice_mage
							trait = eldritch_scholar
							trait = veteran_wizard
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							trait = novice_mage
							trait = eldritch_scholar
							trait = veteran_wizard
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.41 }
				}
			}
			400 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.15
					OR = {
						trait = summoner
						trait = alchemist
						trait = enchanter
						trait = herbalist
						trait = necromancer
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					lifestyle_traits = 1
					has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							trait = summoner
							trait = alchemist
							trait = enchanter
							trait = herbalist
							trait = necromancer
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.42 }
				}
			}
			85 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = proud
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { trait = proud }
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.43 }
				}
			}
			85 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = ambitious
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { trait = ambitious }
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.44 }
				}
			}
			85 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = chaste
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { trait = chaste }
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.45 }
				}
			}
			85 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = diligent
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.46 }
				}
			}
			85 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					OR = {
						trait = cynical
						trait = zealous
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							trait = cynical
							trait = zealous
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.47 }
				}
			}
			85 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = erudite
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { trait = erudite }
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.48 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.41 - Improve Education
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.41
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.41
	picture = GFX_evt_relaxed_ruler
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		if = {
			limit = { trait = veteran_wizard }
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = veteran_wizard }
			add_trait = arcane_master
			update_natural_magic = yes
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { trait = eldritch_scholar }
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = eldritch_scholar }
			add_trait = veteran_wizard
			update_natural_magic = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = novice_mage }
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = novice_mage }
			add_trait = eldritch_scholar
			update_natural_magic = yes
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.42 - Gain Progress
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.42
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.42
	picture = GFX_evt_relaxed_ruler
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hide_from = yes
	hide_new = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			# Already maxed out
			AND = {
				lifestyle_traits = 1
				has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			}
			# Alchemy has to complete through a chain
			AND = {
				has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
				has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
			has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
			has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
			has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
				NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration }
				add_trait = summoner
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism }
				add_trait = herbalist
			}
			# Alchemist has its own special end chain instead of this.
			#if = {
			#	limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy }
			#	add_trait = alchemist
			#}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery }
				add_trait = enchanter
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy }
				add_trait = necromancer
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = magic_study_1 }
			remove_character_modifier = magic_study_1
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = magic_study_2
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_modifier = magic_study_1
					has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
					trait = summoner
					trait = alchemist
					trait = enchanter
					trait = herbalist
					trait = necromancer
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				modifier = magic_study_1
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

			NOR = {
				religion_group = christian
				religion_group = muslim
				religion_group = jewish_group
			}

	}

		NOR = {
			trait = necromancer
			has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		}
		piety = 300
		NOT = { trait = cynical }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				trait = crusader
				trait = mujahid
				trait = shaddai
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = ashari
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			trait = mutazilite
		}
		modifier = {

			OR = {
				trait = sayyid
				trait = mirza
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = decadent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_character_modifier = voice_of_jesus
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_character_modifier = voice_of_satan
		}
		modifier = {

			trait = excommunicated

		modifier = {

			}

			trait = erudite

				trait = eldritch_scholar

				trait = arcane_master
			}
		}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.57
		add_trait = miracle_worker
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.57
		trigger = { ai = no }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOR = {
					trait = humble
					trait = proud
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				add_trait = humble
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = 38260 }
				}
			}
		}
		piety = 30
	}
}

				trait = blinded
			}
		}

			}
		}

}

# MYTH_WoL.59 - Completion of Books of Hermes
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.59
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.59
	picture = GFX_evt_squaring_the_circle
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	
	trigger = {
		has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy # In case study focus was changed - can't use this as a shortcut for another path
		has_character_modifier = reading_books_hermes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.59
		remove_character_modifier = reading_books_hermes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = { # Already as far as this reward goes normally
					has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
					trait = alchemist
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1} }
		}
		else = {
			#limit = {
			#	NOR = {
			#		has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			#		trait = alchemist
			#	}
			#}
			add_character_modifier = { name = magic_study_2 duration = -1 }
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.61 - Possible religious conversion when reading Books of Hermes
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.61
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.61
	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	capable_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_character_modifier = reading_books_hermes
		true_religion_group = pagan_group
		is_monotheistic = no
		NOT = {	trait = blinded }
		prisoner = no
	}
	
	# Convert to Christianity
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.61
		random_list = {
			40 = { religion = catholic }
			40 = { religion = orthodox }
			9 = { religion = miaphysite }
			9 = { religion = nestorian }
			2 = { religion = messalian }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				region = world_europe
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.61
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_dlc = "The Sword of Islam" # Don't let a player game over themself
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			45 = { religion = sunni }
			45 = { religion = shiite }
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					year = 1066
				}
				religion = ibadi
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					region = world_middle_east
					region = world_africa
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.61
		religion = zoroastrian
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "The Old Gods" # With Holy Fury, it's now possible to be able to play pagans but not zoroastrians
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				region = world_persia
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.61
		if = {
			limit = { trait = zealous }
			piety = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = cynical } }
			add_trait = zealous
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = cynical }
			remove_trait = cynical
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
}

		NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
	}

		days = 1

			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
				has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
			}
		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {

			wealth = 500
		}

		}
	}

	}

# MYTH_WoL.66 - Phase 2

	id = MYTH_WoL.66
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.66

			limit = {

					prisoner = yes

					lifestyle_traits = 1
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy }

# MYTH_WoL.67 - Check success or failure
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.67
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = failed_alchemy }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.68 }
			break = yes
		}
		# Success! Now purify the metal to determine how well you are rewarded
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.69 }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.69 - Purify the metal to determine rewards
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.69
	title = EVTNAMEMYTH_WoL.69
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.69
	picture = GFX_evt_squaring_the_circle
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# See if you're no longer eligable. If so, clear flag and stop the event
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					prisoner = yes
					#trait = incapable
					is_incapable = yes
					lifestyle_traits = 1
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy }
				}
			}
			break = yes
		}
	}
	
	# Aqua Regia has a special failure, which just ends up repeating the event
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.69
		hidden_tooltip = {	character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.70 days = 1 } }
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
	# Aqua Fortis - Gaurenteed success, but poor rewards
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.69
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.71 days = 2 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = greedy
			}
		}
	}
	# Mercury - Scales with Magic training
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.69
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					# Failure
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.72 days = 4 }
				}
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = novice_mage
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = eldritch_scholar
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.5
						trait = veteran_wizard
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						trait = arcane_master
					}
					# Success
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.73 days = 4 }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPCMYTH_WoL.69 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					trait = novice_mage
					trait = eldritch_scholar
					trait = veteran_wizard
					trait = arcane_master
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.69
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = lustful
					}
					modifier = { 
						factor = 1.1
						trait = gluttonous
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = greedy
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = slothful
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = envious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = wroth
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = proud
					}
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.70 days = 7 }
				}
				30 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = detached_priest
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = martial_cleric
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.5
						trait = scholarly_theologian
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						trait = mastermind_theologian
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						piety = 500
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						piety = 1000
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						piety = 2000
					}

						factor = 1.1
						trait = chaste
					}

					}

					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = kind
					}
					modifier = {

						trait = patient
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = humble
					}

# MYTH_WoL.81 - Spin straw into gold
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.81
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.81
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
		trait = lunatic
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
				trait = lunatic
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.81
		hidden_tooltip = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = trait
				novice_mage = {
					random_list = {
						50 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.82 days = 1 } }
						50 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.83 days = 1 } }
					}
				}
				eldritch_scholar = {
					random_list = {
						55 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.82 days = 1 } }
						45 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.83 days = 1 } }
					}
				}
				veteran_wizard = {
					random_list = {
						60 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.82 days = 1 } }
						40 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.83 days = 1 } }
					}
				}
				arcane_master = {
					random_list = {
						65 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.82 days = 1 } }
						35 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.83 days = 1 } }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						trait = novice_mage
						trait = eldritch_scholar
						trait = veteran_wizard
						trait = arcane_master
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					30 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.82 days = 1 } }
					70 = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.83 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.84 - Create illusionary castle defenders
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.84
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.84
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_rulers = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
		NOT = { trait = honest }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_province_flag = crown_focus_province }
			}							
			save_event_target_as = random_province
		}
		any_demesne_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = crown_focus_province }
			save_event_target_as = crown_focus
		}
	}
	
	# Target Capital
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.84
		capital_scope = {
			any_province_holding = {
				add_holding_modifier = { modifier = illusionary_defenders years = 1 stacking = no }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 } }
	}
	# Crown Focus
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.84
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "Reapers"
			any_demesne_province = {
				has_province_flag = crown_focus_province
			}
			NOT = { capital_scope = { province = event_target:crown_focus } }
		}
		event_target:crown_focus = {
			any_province_holding = {
				add_holding_modifier = { modifier = illusionary_defenders years = 1 stacking = no }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 } }
	}
	# Random Province
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.84

# MYTH_WoL.85 - Practice Shapeshifting
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.85
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.85
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			score_value = {
				value = 10
				interesting_courtier_selection_score = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = stalked
		}
	}
	
	# Tail someone and learn their secrets
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.85
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TT_find_stalked_secrets
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:stalked = {
				random_list = {
					# Sexual proclivities
					5 = {
						trigger = {
							OR = {
								trait = homosexual
								trait = hedonist
								trait = syphilitic
								trait = seducer
								trait = seductress
								AND = {
									is_married = no
									num_of_lovers = 1
									has_concubinage = no # If they allow concubines, they probably don't care too much about fornication
								}
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							trait = celibate
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.2
							trait = chaste
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							trait = lustful
						}
						ROOT = {
							set_character_flag = reason_sexual
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					# Secret lover
					5 = {
						trigger = {
							is_married = yes
							any_lover = {
								NOT = {
									any_spouse = {
										character = PREVPREV
									}
								}
								is_abroad = no
								prisoner = no
								NOT = { trait = incapable }
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
							}
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.2
							trait = chaste
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 2
							trait = lustful
						}
						ROOT = {
							set_character_flag = reason_lover
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					# Secret Religion
					5 = {
						trigger = {
							has_secret_religion = yes
							religion = ROOT
							NOT = { ROOT = { has_prevs_secret_religion_truly_trigger = yes } }
						}
						ROOT = {
							set_character_flag = reason_religion
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					# Secret Society
					5 = {
						trigger = {
							is_in_society = yes
							NOT = { same_society_as = ROOT }
							OR = {
								society_is_criminal = yes
								AND = {
									society_is_devil_worshiper = yes
									religion = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							set_character_flag = reason_society
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					# Secret Werewolf
					5 = {
						trigger = {
							trait = secret_werewolf
							ROOT = {
								NOR = { 
									trait = werewolf
									culture = werewolf_culture
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							set_character_flag = reason_werewolf
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					# Secret Vampire
					5 = {
						trigger = {
							trait = secret_vampire
							ROOT = {
								NOR = { 
									trait = vampire
									culture = vampire_culture
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							set_character_flag = reason_vampire
							character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.197 days = 3 }
						}
					}
					# Nothing found
					10 = {
						additive_modifier = {
							value = 2
							intrigue = 10
						}
						additive_modifier = {
							value = 2
							intrigue = 15
						}
						additive_modifier = {
							value = 2
							intrigue = 20
						}
						additive_modifier = {
							value = 2
							intrigue = 25
						}
						additive_modifier = {
							value = 2
							intrigue = 30
						}

							value = -2
							ROOT = { intrigue = 10 }
						}

							value = -2
							ROOT = { intrigue = 15 }
						}

							value = -2

							value = -2

							factor = 1.2

						}

						}

			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5

				factor = 2
				trait = deceitful
			}

				factor = 2
				trait = paranoid
			}

# MYTH_WoL.86 - Weather Control
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.86
	picture = GFX_evt_library
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.86
		picture = GFX_evt_prospering_province
		trigger = {
			has_dlc = "Reapers"
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.86
		picture = GFX_evt_library
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		OR = {
			trait = novice_mage
			trait = eldritch_scholar
			trait = veteran_wizard
			trait = arcane_master
		}
	}
		
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_capital = no
				NOT = { has_province_flag = crown_focus_province }
			}							
			save_event_target_as = random_province
		}
		any_demesne_province = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = crown_focus_province }
			save_event_target_as = crown_focus
		}
	}
	
	# Target Capital
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.86
		capital_scope = {
			add_province_modifier = { modifier = bountiful_harvest years = 1 stacking = no }
			custom_tooltip = { text = capital_prospers_custom_tooltip }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { ROOT = { culture_group = undead_culture_group } } }
				hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 6 } }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -6 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 } }
	}
	# Crown Focus
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.86
		trigger = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				has_province_flag = crown_focus_province
			}
			capital_scope = {
				NOT = { province = event_target:crown_focus }
			}
		}
		event_target:crown_focus = {
			add_province_modifier = { modifier = bountiful_harvest years = 1 stacking = no }
			custom_tooltip = { text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { ROOT = { culture_group = undead_culture_group } } }
				hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 6 } }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -6 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 } }
	}
	# Random Province
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.86
		#trigger = {
		#	event_target:random_province = {
		#		always = true
		#	}
		#}
		trigger = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				NOT = { has_province_flag = crown_focus_province }
				NOT = { ROOT = { capital_scope = { province = PREVPREV } } }
			}
		}
				
		event_target:random_province = {
			add_province_modifier = { modifier = bountiful_harvest years = 1 stacking = no }
			custom_tooltip = { text = increase_prosperity_custom_tooltip }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { ROOT = { culture_group = undead_culture_group } } }
				hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 6 } }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = -6 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 } }
	}
	# None
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.86
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
	}
}

			is_ill = yes
		}

		days = 1

			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
				any_courtier = {
					is_ill = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

			limit = { is_ill = yes }

				interesting_courtier_selection_score = yes

		}
	}

# MYTH_WoL.90 - Actually run the healing event
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.90
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.90
	picture = GFX_evt_illness
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_herb_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_animal_part_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_powder_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_liquid_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.90
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.91 days = 1 } } }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPMYTH_WoL.90 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.90
		tooltip_info = yes
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPMYTH_WoL.90 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { selected_ingredient_is_perceived_healthy_trigger = yes }
				FROM = { set_character_flag = recieve_potion_good }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { selected_ingredient_is_unhealthy_trigger = yes }
				FROM = { set_character_flag = recieve_potion_bad }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { selected_ingredient_is_perceived_healthy_trigger = yes }
				FROM = { set_character_flag = potion_looks_good }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { selected_ingredient_is_unhealthy_trigger = yes }
				FROM = { set_character_flag = potion_looks_bad }
			}
			FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.91 days = 1 } }
		}
		destroy_selected_ingredient_1_effect = yes

        trigger = {
        	any_artifact = {
        		has_artifact_flag = ingredient
        	}
        }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.90
		trigger = {
			ai = no 
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.105
		trigger = {
			trait = dragon
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPAMYTH_WoL.105 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = loop_control value = 1 }
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { which = loop_control value = 0 } }
				random = {
					chance = 60
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						trait = novice_mage
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						trait = eldritch_scholar
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.6
						trait = veteran_wizard
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.8
						trait = arcane_master
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						OR = {
							# Birds are alchemical symbols representing the creation of the philosopher's stone
							has_character_modifier = owl_familiar
							has_character_modifier = dove_familiar
							has_character_modifier = raven_familiar
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning = 5
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						learning = 10
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1

					}

				}
				subtract_variable = { which = loop_control value = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.106 days = 5 random = 2 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}

# MYTH_WoL.108 - Determine alchemical success
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.108
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# One last chance for success
		random = {
			chance = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = novice_mage
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				trait = eldritch_scholar
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.6
				trait = veteran_wizard
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.8
				trait = arcane_master
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				OR = {
					# Birds are alchemical symbols representing the creation of the philosopher's stone
					has_character_modifier = owl_familiar
					has_character_modifier = dove_familiar
					has_character_modifier = raven_familiar
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 30
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 35
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 40
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				learning = 45
			}
			change_variable = { which = num_successes value = 1 }
		}
		
		# Determine full success
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = num_successes value = 7 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.109 }
		}
		# Partial failure
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = num_successes value = 4 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.110 }
		}
		# Complete failure
		else = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.111 }
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.109 - Formed Philosopher's Stone
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.109
	title = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.109
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.109
	picture = GFX_evt_squaring_the_circle
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.109
		remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
		add_trait = alchemist
		add_artifact = philosopher_stone
		add_trait = philosopher_stone_trait
		prestige = 1000
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = magic_bloodline
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_religion_feature = religion_matriarchal
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = BL_alchemist
					inheritance = matrilineal
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_religion_feature = religion_equal
						has_religion_feature = religion_feature_bon
						culture = basque
						culture = zhangzhung
						culture = sumpa
						religion = cathar
						religion = messalian
						religion = mazdaki
					}
				}
				create_bloodline = {
					type = BL_alchemist
					inheritance = all_descendants
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_bloodline = {
					type = BL_alchemist
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { can_apply_cool_nickname_trigger = yes }
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						NOT = { age = 30 }
						can_apply_lame_nickname_trigger = yes
					}
					give_nickname = nick_the_youthful
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { can_apply_average_nickname_trigger = yes }
					give_nickname = nick_the_wealthy
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { can_apply_cool_nickname_trigger = yes }
					give_nickname = nick_the_undying
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { can_apply_lame_nickname_trigger = yes }
					give_nickname = nick_the_scholar
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { can_apply_cool_nickname_trigger = yes }
					give_nickname = the_wizard
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { can_apply_cool_nickname_trigger = yes }
					give_nickname = nick_the_alchemist
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		NAND = {
			trait = stressed
			trait = depressed
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = eldritch_scholar
				trait = veteran_wizard
				trait = arcane_master
				trait = dull
				trait = slow
				trait = imbecile
				trait = inbred
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.115
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			add_trait = depressed
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = stressed
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.128 - Begin tower construction
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.128
	title = EVTNAMEMYTH_WoL.128
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.128
	picture = GFX_evt_magnificent_castle
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_capable = yes
	only_playable = yes
	has_dlc = "Way of Life"
	min_age = 16
	only_independent = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		OR = {
			trait = summoner
			trait = enchanter
			trait = alchemist
			trait = herbalist
			trait = necromancer
			AND = {
				has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
				NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				OR = {
					has_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
					has_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
					has_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
					has_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
					has_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
					has_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
					has_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
					has_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
					has_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
					has_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { tier = baron }
		capital_holding = {
			OR = {
				holding_type = castle
				holding_type = city
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 0 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.128
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.4 min = -30 max = -300 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.128 }
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			change_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 1 }
			random = {
				chance = 10
				change_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.130 days = 30 random = 25 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				check_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				check_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				check_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				check_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				trait = architect
			}
			# No second expansion
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.187 }
			break = yes
		}
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.135 }
	}
}
