# MYTH_WoL.139 - Complete tower
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.139
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.139
	picture = GFX_evt_magnificent_castle
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration }
			set_character_flag = build_conjuration
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism }
			set_character_flag = build_herbalism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy }
			set_character_flag = build_alchemy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery }
			set_character_flag = build_enchantment
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy }
			set_character_flag = build_necromancy
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.139
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = magic_study_2 }
			remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration }
				add_trait = summoner
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism }
				add_trait = herbalist
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy }
				add_trait = alchemist
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery }
				add_trait = enchanter
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy }
				add_trait = necromancer
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = build_enchantment }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = build_conjuration }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = build_alchemy }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = build_herbalism }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = build_necromancy }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_scrying_room }
			clr_character_flag = built_scrying_room
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = scrying_chamber duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_room_of_portals }
			clr_character_flag = built_room_of_portals
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = room_of_portal duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_gold_tower }
			clr_character_flag = built_gold_tower
			prestige = 200
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = gold_tower duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_greenhouse }
			clr_character_flag = built_greenhouse
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = greenhouse duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_calming }
			clr_character_flag = built_calming
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = calming_enchantment duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_otherworldly_guard }
			clr_character_flag = built_otherworldly_guard
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = otherworldly_guard duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_alchemist_lab }
			clr_character_flag = built_alchemist_lab
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = alchemist_lab duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_medical_supplies }
			clr_character_flag = built_medical_supplies
			add_artifact = medical_supplies
			hermetic_add_herbal_q2_ingredient_effect = yes
			hermetic_add_herbal_q2_ingredient_effect = yes
			add_artifact = ingredient_asclepois
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_divination_chamber }
			clr_character_flag = built_divination_chamber
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = divination_room duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_tower_crypt }
			clr_character_flag = built_tower_crypt
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = tower_crypt duration = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_character_flag = build_enchantment
		clr_character_flag = build_conjuration
		clr_character_flag = build_alchemy
		clr_character_flag = build_herbalism
		clr_character_flag = build_necromancy
	}
}
# MYTH_WoL.140 - Remove old building
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.140
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.140
	picture = GFX_evt_construction_site
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.140
		scaled_wealth = { value = 0.3 min = 20 max = 200 }
		prestige = -50
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.140 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
					}
				}
				any_province_holding = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
				any_province_holding = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
				remove_province_modifier = room_of_portal
				remove_province_modifier = otherworldly_guard
				remove_province_modifier = scrying_chamber
				remove_province_modifier = calming_enchantment
				remove_province_modifier = gold_tower
				remove_province_modifier = alchemist_lab
				remove_province_modifier = greenhouse
				remove_province_modifier = divination_room
				remove_province_modifier = tower_crypt
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.140
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.142
	picture = GFX_evt_construction_site
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_capable = yes
	only_playable = yes
	has_dlc = "Way of Life"
	min_age = 16
	only_independent = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	# Enchanter
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.131
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.7 min = -10 max = -400 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.131 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = built_scrying_room
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.192 days = 7 }
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = enchanter
				has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.7 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { wealth = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	# Conjurer
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.131
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.4 min = -5 max = -300 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTBMYTH_WoL.131 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = built_room_of_portals
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.192 days = 30 random = 10 }
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = summoner
				has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { wealth = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	# Alchemist
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.131
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTCMYTH_WoL.131 }
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -300 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = built_gold_tower
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.192 days = 90 random = 30 }
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = alchemist
				has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { wealth = 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.15
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
	# Herbalist
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.131
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.3 min = -5 max = -200 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTDMYTH_WoL.131 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = built_greenhouse
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.192 days = 7 }
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = herbalist
				has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { wealth = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Necromancer
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFMYTH_WoL.131
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.2 min = -5 max = -200 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTFMYTH_WoL.131 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = built_divination_chamber
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.184 days = 30 random = 20 }
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = necromancer
				has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				NOT = { scaled_wealth = 0.2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = { wealth = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEMYTH_WoL.131
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.143 days = 3 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}
# MYTH_WoL.143 - Possible delay
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.143
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.132
	picture = GFX_evt_construction_site
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_capable = yes
	only_playable = yes
	has_dlc = "Way of Life"
	min_age = 16
	only_independent = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	# Rush the constuction
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.132
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.132 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random = {
				chance = 70
				subtract_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.144 days = 7 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = patient
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Take all the time you need
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.132
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.132 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				change_variable = { which = tower_quality value = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.144 days = 90 random = 30 }
		}
		trigger = { trait = patient }
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.132
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.132 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.144 days = 45 random = 15 }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.147 - Completed Tower
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.147
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.147
	picture = GFX_evt_magnificent_castle
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.139
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
						has_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
						has_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
					}
				}
				any_province_holding = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
					remove_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
				any_province_holding = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
					remove_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
				remove_province_modifier = room_of_portal
				remove_province_modifier = otherworldly_guard
				remove_province_modifier = scrying_chamber
				remove_province_modifier = calming_enchantment
				remove_province_modifier = gold_tower
				remove_province_modifier = alchemist_lab
				remove_province_modifier = greenhouse
				remove_province_modifier = divination_room
				remove_province_modifier = tower_crypt
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { trait = enchanter }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_enchantment
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_enchantment
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = summoner }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_conjuration
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_conjuration
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = alchemist }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_alchemy
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_alchemy
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = herbalist }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_herbalism
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_herbalism
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = necromancer }
			capital_holding = {
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = castle }
					add_building = ca_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
				if = {
					limit = { holding_type = city }
					add_building = ct_mage_tower_necromancy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_scrying_room }
			clr_character_flag = built_scrying_room
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = scrying_chamber duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_room_of_portals }
			clr_character_flag = built_room_of_portals
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = room_of_portal duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_gold_tower }
			clr_character_flag = built_gold_tower
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = gold_tower duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_gold_tower }
			clr_character_flag = built_gold_tower
			prestige = 200
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = gold_tower duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_greenhouse }
			clr_character_flag = built_greenhouse
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = greenhouse duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_calming }
			clr_character_flag = built_calming
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = calming_enchantment duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_otherworldly_guard }
			clr_character_flag = built_otherworldly_guard
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = otherworldly_guard duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_alchemist_lab }
			clr_character_flag = built_alchemist_lab
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = alchemist_lab duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_medical_supplies }
			clr_character_flag = built_medical_supplies
			add_artifact = medical_supplies
			hermetic_add_herbal_q2_ingredient_effect = yes
			hermetic_add_herbal_q2_ingredient_effect = yes
			add_artifact = ingredient_asclepois
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_divination_chamber }
			clr_character_flag = built_divination_chamber
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = divination_room duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = built_tower_crypts }
			clr_character_flag = built_tower_crypts
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { modifier = tower_crypt duration = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.148 - Weather focus loader so it doesn't always pick the same province
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.148
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_rulers = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		OR = {
			trait = novice_mage
			trait = eldritch_scholar
			trait = veteran_wizard
			trait = arcane_master
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOR = {
				has_focus = focus_magic
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = eldritch_scholar
				trait = veteran_wizard
				trait = arcane_master
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				trait = kind
				trait = gluttonous
				trait = greedy
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			trait = charitable
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		#random_demesne_province = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_capital = no
		#		NOT = { has_province_flag = crown_focus_province }
		#	}							
		#	save_event_target_as = random_province
		#}
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.86 days = 1 }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.149 - Test forest herbs
character_event = {
	id = "MYTH_WoL.149"
	desc = "EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.149"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunting_scene
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_rulers = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.149
		random_list = {
			50 = {
			}
			30 = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = tt_gain_ingredient
					hidden_tooltip = { hermetic_add_herbal_q1_ingredient_effect = yes }
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					NOT = { learning = 8 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					NOT = { learning = 5 }
				}
				change_learning = 1
				hermetic_add_herbal_q1_ingredient_effect = yes
			}
			10 = {
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPMYTH_WoL.149 }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					give_food_poisoning_effect = yes
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					learning = 5
				}
				add_trait = food_poisoning
				death = { death_reason = death_trait }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.149
	}
}
# MYTH_WoL.150 - Trigger for regular Evocatio.  Want a slight delay, want ROOT to be Roman/Hellenic side
# No longer used - MYTH_WoL.152 is called from fire_haruspicy_event_effect
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.150
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = hellenic_pagan_reformed
					religion = hellenic_pagan
				}
				FROM = {
					NOR = {
						religion = hellenic_pagan_reformed
						religion = hellenic_pagan
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { save_event_target_as = non_roman_side }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.152 days = 1 }
			break = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					religion = hellenic_pagan_reformed
					religion = hellenic_pagan
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						religion = hellenic_pagan_reformed
						religion = hellenic_pagan
					}
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = non_roman_war_side
			FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.152 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

		else_if = {

					religion = hellenic_pagan
				}
				FROM = {
					holder_scope = {
						OR = {

					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

# MYTH_WoL.152 - Evocatio (Latin) or Anaklesis (Greek) - not really a greek thing, but seemed better than leaving it in Latin for them.
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.152
	picture = GFX_evt_rome_restored_byzantine
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCAMYTH_WoL.152
		trigger = { religion = hellenic_pagan }
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCBMYTH_WoL.152
		trigger = { religion = hellenic_pagan_reformed }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		# Should already be at war and hellenic or roman from how this triggers
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
		piety = 100
	}
	
	# Sacrifice for ritual
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.152
		scaled_wealth = { value = -0.3 min = 10 max = 500 }
		random_list = {
			70 = {
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.152 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.153 days = 3 } }
			}
			30 = {
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTBMYTH_WoL.152 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.154 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Perform the ritual
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.152
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTAMYTH_WoL.152 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.153 days = 3 } }
			}
			50 = {
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTTBMYTH_WoL.152 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.154 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Don't Perform the ritual
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.152
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = zealous } }
			random = {
				chance = 20
				add_trait = cynical
				hidden_tooltip = {
					# Notify
					character_event = { id = 38258 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			#limit = { trait = zealous }
			random = {
				chance = 33
				remove_trait = zealous
				hidden_tooltip = {
					# Notify
					character_event = { id = 38310 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.158 - control results of search for GKoS
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.158
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		NOT = { has_artifact = greater_key_of_solomon }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.159 days = 60 random = 30 } # Nothing found
			}
			10 = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.160 days = 30 random = 15 } # Library of local noble
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							any_vassal = {
								num_of_count_titles = 1
							}
						}
						NOT = { has_dlc = Zeus }
					}
				}
			}
			10 = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.162 days = 45 random = 15 } # Library of a foreign noble
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					NOT = { scaled_wealth = 1 }
				}
			}
			10 = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.163 days = 20 random = 10 } # Held by bastard
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						any_child = {
							trait = bastard
							age = 16
						}
					}
				}
			}
			10 = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.165 days = 50 random = 25 } # Held in church reliquary
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = {
						religion_group = christian
						religion = satanist
						religion = hindu
						religion = buddhist
					}
				}
			}
			10 = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.166 days = 30 random = 15 } # Held by heretic/infidel liege
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					liege = {
						OR = {
							religion = ROOT
							NOT = { trait = zealous }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.163 - In private collection of bastard
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.163
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.162
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		NOT = { has_artifact = greater_key_of_solomon }
		any_child = {
			trait = bastard
			age = 16
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				trait = bastard
				age = 16
			}
			save_event_target_as = kos_vassal
			export_to_variable = { which = age_compare value = age }
		}
		current_heir = {
			export_to_variable = { which = age_compare value = age }
			subtract_variable = { which = age_compare which = kos_vassal }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.163
		add_artifact = greater_key_of_solomon
		new_artifact = {
			set_creation_date = 1.1.1
		}
		event_target:kos_vassal = {
			remove_trait = bastard
			add_trait = legit_bastard
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 }
			event_target:kos_vassal = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.164 } }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.167 days = 10 random = 2 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_law = succ_gavelkind
					has_law = succ_elective_gavelkind
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				event_target:kos_vassal = { is_female = yes }
				OR = {
					has_law = agnatic_succession
					has_law = cognatic_succession
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				event_target:kos_vassal = { is_female = no }
				OR = {
					has_law = enatic_succession
					has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				event_target:kos_vassal = { is_female = no }
				OR = {
					has_law = agnatic_succession
					has_law = cognatic_succession
				}
				current_heir = { is_female = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				event_target:kos_vassal = { is_female = yes }
				OR = {
					has_law = enatic_succession
					has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
				}
				current_heir = { is_female = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					has_law = succ_seniority
					has_law = succ_primogeniture
				}
				OR = {
					event_target:kos_vassal = { is_female = no }
					has_law = true_cognatic_succession
					has_law = enatic_succession
					has_law = enatic_cognatic_succession
				}
				current_heir = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = age_compare value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.163
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.190 - Handle educationless adulthood, with slight delay via bounce to avoid double-education
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.190
	picture = GFX_evt_noble_in_castle
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_diplomacy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCB_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_martial
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCC_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_stewardship
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCD_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_intrigue
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCE_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_learning
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCF_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_magic
		}
	}
	
	trigger = { # Make sure we have no education focus and no education outcome already set
		has_dlc = "Zeus"
		NOR = {
			has_character_flag = is_being_graded
			has_focus = focus_ed_diplomacy
			has_focus = focus_ed_martial
			has_focus = focus_ed_stewardship
			has_focus = focus_ed_intrigue
			has_focus = focus_ed_learning
			has_focus = focus_ed_magic
			trait = naive_appeaser
			trait = underhanded_rogue
			trait = charismatic_negotiator
			trait = grey_eminence
			trait = misguided_warrior
			trait = tough_soldier
			trait = skilled_tactician
			trait = brilliant_strategist
			trait = indulgent_wastrel
			trait = thrifty_clerk
			trait = fortune_builder
			trait = midas_touched
			trait = amateurish_plotter
			trait = flamboyant_schemer
			trait = intricate_webweaver
			trait = elusive_shadow
			trait = detached_priest
			trait = martial_cleric
			trait = scholarly_theologian
			trait = mastermind_theologian
			trait = novice_mage
			trait = eldritch_scholar
			trait = veteran_wizard
			trait = arcane_master
		}
		NOT ={
			has_character_flag = is_child_of_destiny
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		educator = { save_event_target_as = education_outcome_educator }
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				set_character_flag = education_diplomacy
			}
			10 = {
				set_character_flag = education_martial
			}
			10 = {
				set_character_flag = education_stewardship
			}
			10 = {
				set_character_flag = education_intrigue
			}
			10 = {
				set_character_flag = education_learning
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = pagan_group
						religion = satanist
						trait = possessed
						trait = mystic
						trait = enchanter
						trait = summoner
						trait = herbalist
						trait = alchemist
						trait = blood_of_the_gods
						any_owned_bloodline = { has_bloodline_flag = BOTG }
						trait = dragon
						trait = dragonborn
						trait = djinn
						trait = demi_god
						trait = god
						trait = demon_trait
						trait = magic_heritage
						father_even_if_dead = {
							OR = {
								trait = novice_mage
								trait = eldritch_scholar
								trait = veteran_wizard
								trait = arcane_master
							}
						}
						mother_even_if_dead = {
							OR = {
								trait = novice_mage
								trait = eldritch_scholar
								trait = veteran_wizard
								trait = arcane_master
							}
						}
						guardian = {
							OR = {
								trait = novice_mage
								trait = eldritch_scholar
								trait = veteran_wizard
								trait = arcane_master
							}
						}
						educator = {
							OR = {
								trait = novice_mage
								trait = eldritch_scholar
								trait = veteran_wizard
								trait = arcane_master
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = education_magic
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = education_effect_imprisoned
		clr_character_flag = was_willful
		clr_character_flag = was_brooding
		clr_character_flag = was_indolent
		clr_character_flag = was_playful
		clr_character_flag = was_conscientious
		clr_character_flag = was_fussy
		clr_character_flag = was_curious
		clr_character_flag = was_idolizer
		clr_character_flag = was_haughty
		clr_character_flag = was_affectionate
		clr_character_flag = was_timid
		clr_character_flag = was_rowdy
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_diplomacy
		}
		add_trait = naive_appeaser
		clr_character_flag = education_diplomacy
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_martial
		}
		add_trait = misguided_warrior
		clr_character_flag = education_martial
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_stewardship
		}
		add_trait = indulgent_wastrel
		clr_character_flag = education_stewardship
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_intrigue
		}
		add_trait = amateurish_plotter
		clr_character_flag = education_intrigue
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_learning
		}
		add_trait = detached_priest
		clr_character_flag = education_learning
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_ZE_14700
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = education_magic
		}
		add_trait = novice_mage
		update_natural_magic = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = magic_heritage } }
			add_trait = magic_heritage
		}
		clr_character_flag = education_learning
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			# Notify educator
			event_target:education_outcome_educator = { character_event = { id = ZE.14710 } } 
			if = {
				limit = { # Notify mother if primary heir
					mother = {
						event_target:education_outcome_educator = {
							NOT = { character = PREV }
						}
						ROOT = {
							is_primary_heir = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				mother = {
					character_event = { id = ZE.14710 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { # Notify father if primary heir
					father = {
						event_target:education_outcome_educator = {
							NOT = { character = PREV }
						}
						ROOT = {
							is_primary_heir = PREV
						}
					} 
				}
				father = {
					character_event = { id = ZE.14710 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Control for finishing reading book of hermes
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.195
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy # In case study focus was changed - can't use this as a shortcut for another path
		has_character_modifier = reading_books_hermes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = blinded #  Can't read
				trait = werewolf # but can heal from it
			}
			repeat_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.195 days = 30 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					#trait = incapable # Unlikely to ever have a chance to fire again
					is_incapable = yes
					trait = blinded # Already covered main way of curing this
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy } # Changed area of study
				}
			}
			remove_character_modifier = reading_books_hermes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				prisoner = yes # Can't complete in prison, check again if released
			}
			repeat_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.195 days = 30 }
		}
		else = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.59 }
		}
	}
}

# Make Zeus seduce someone else, outside of current court
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.196
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	only_men = yes
	only_capable = yes
	has_dlc = "Way of Life"
	ai = yes
	has_character_flag = greek_god_zeus
		
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_seduction
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Remove current seduction target
		random_opinion_modifier_target = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						modifier = opinion_seducing
					}
				}
			}
			reverse_remove_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_seducing
			}
			
			clear_delayed_event = { id = WoL.110 }
		
			clr_character_flag = wol_seduce_love_letter
			clr_character_flag = wol_seduce_gift
			clr_character_flag = wol_seduce_gossip
			clr_character_flag = wol_seduce_dance
			clr_character_flag = wol_seduce_chance_meeting
			clr_character_flag = wol_seduce_picnic
			clr_character_flag = seduction_confirmed
		}
		
		# Seduce someone new
		random_character = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_lover = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_former_lover = ROOT }
				
				NOT = { is_consort = ROOT }
				NOT = { any_spouse = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { same_sex = ROOT }
				NOT = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { same_liege = ROOT }
				NOT = { at_location = ROOT }
				NOR = {
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_seduced_refused }
					has_character_modifier = dismissed_proposal
				}
				NOT = { trait = celibate }
				religion_group = ROOT
				is_within_diplo_range = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				opinion = {
					who = PREV
					modifier = opinion_seducing
					years = 1000
				}
				character_event = { id = WoL.100 days = 1 } # No warning - Let the chase begin!
			}
		}
	}
}

# Found someone's secrets while transformed
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.197
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_sexual
			NOT = { event_target:stalked = { trait = homosexual } }
		}
		text = EVTDESCAMYTH_WoL.197
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_lover
			NOT = { event_target:stalked = { trait = homosexual } }
		}
		text = EVTDESCBMYTH_WoL.197
		picture = GFX_evt_lovers
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_religion
		}
		text = EVTDESCCMYTH_WoL.197
		picture = GFX_evt_secluded_in_prayer
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_society
		}
		text = EVTDESCDMYTH_WoL.197
		picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_werewolf
		}
		text = EVTDESCEMYTH_WoL.197
		picture = GFX_evt_werewolf_shadowed
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_vampire
		}
		text = EVTDESCFMYTH_WoL.197
		picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_sexual
			event_target:stalked = { trait = homosexual }
		}
		text = EVTDESCGMYTH_WoL.197
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_lover
			event_target:stalked = { trait = homosexual }
		}
		text = EVTDESCBMYTH_WoL.197
		picture = GFX_evt_lovers
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = reason_sexual
					has_character_flag = reason_lover
				}
				event_target:stalked = { trait = homosexual }
			}
			opinion = { who = event_target:stalked modifier = opinion_discovered_homosexual years = -1 }
		}
	}
	
	# Blackmail them
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.197
		event_target:stalked = { 
			# Going to wipe ROOT's flags at the end of this event, so set flags on stalked
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_sexual } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_sexual
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_lover } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_lover
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_religion } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_religion
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_society } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_society
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_werewolf } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_vampire } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_vampire
			}
			letter_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.199 days = 2 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = ambitious
			}
		}
	}
	# Inform their spouse
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.197
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_lover
		}
		event_target:stalked = {
			spouse = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.202 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = shy
			}
		}
	}
	# Expose them!
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.197
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = reason_werewolf
				has_character_flag = reason_vampire
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = reason_sexual
						has_character_flag = reason_lover
					}
					trait = homosexual
					NOT = { any_lover = { character = ROOT } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = reason_werewolf }
			
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = event_target:stalked
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
		
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_MYTH_WoL.9 }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				event_target:stalked = { 
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.6 } # Character uncovered as a werewolf
					save_event_target_as = target_discovered_werewolf
				}
				any_realm_character = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.7 } } # Court finds out character is a werewolf
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { event_target:stalked = { liege = { character = ROOT } } }
					}
					event_target:stalked = { liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.8 } } } # Liege finds out character is a werewolf
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = reason_vampire }
			
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = event_target:stalked
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
			
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_VAMPIRE.17 }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				event_target:stalked = {
					character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.14 }# Character uncovered as a vampire
					save_event_target_as = target_discovered_vampire
				}
				any_realm_character = { character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.15 } } # Court finds out character is a vampire
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { event_target:stalked = { liege = { character = ROOT } } }
					}
					event_target:stalked = { liege = { character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.16 } } } # Liege finds out character is a vampire
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = reason_sexual
					has_character_flag = reason_lover
				}
				event_target:stalked = { trait = homosexual }
			}
			
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = event_target:stalked
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
			event_target:stalked = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.203 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = monster_hunter
				NOR = {
					has_character_flag = reason_sexual
					has_character_flag = reason_lover
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
	}
	# Arrest them!
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.197
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_character_flag = reason_sexual
				has_character_flag = reason_lover
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			imprison = event_target:stalked
		}
		event_target:stalked = { 
			# Going to wipe ROOT's flags at the end of this event, so set flags on stalked
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_sexual } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_sexual
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_lover } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_lover
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_religion } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_religion
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_society } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_society
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_werewolf } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = reason_vampire } }
				set_character_flag = exposed_vampire
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.204 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = monster_hunter
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = reason_werewolf
					has_character_flag = reason_vampire
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 # Not the reason for the arrest, but you want to lock them up anyway
				trait = monster_hunter
				event_target:stalked = {
					is_monster_to_root = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
		}
	}
	# Demand breakup
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEMYTH_WoL.197
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = reason_lover
			any_spouse = { character = event_target:stalked }
		}
		event_target:stalked = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.205 }

		name = EVTOPTFMYTH_WoL.197
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}

				trait = arbitrary
			}

		clr_character_flag = reason_lover

	}

				has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction }

	desc = {

			has_character_flag = exposed_vampire

				is_landed = no
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction }
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESCNMYTH_WoL.199
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Accept - stay out of factions
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.199
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_pleased
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_landed = yes
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction } }
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_coerced_into_leaving_faction
				who = FROM
				months = 1200
			}
		}
		else = {
			tooltip = {
				transfer_scaled_wealth = { to = FROM value = 0.3 }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clr_character_flag = exposed_sexual
			clr_character_flag = exposed_lover
			clr_character_flag = exposed_religion
			clr_character_flag = exposed_society
			clr_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
			clr_character_flag = exposed_vampire
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.200 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 5.0
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = trusting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
				liege = {
					NOR = {
						culture = werewolf_culture
						trait = werewolf
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_character_flag = exposed_vampire
				liege = {
					NOR = {
						culture = vampire_culture
						trait = vampire
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.199
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_slandered
			months = 24
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.201 } }
		}
		
		tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_sexual }
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = opinion_charge_deviant
					months = 24
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = homosexual
					is_female = no
					NOR = {
						has_character_modifier = known_sodomite
						has_character_modifier = known_sodomite_pagan
					}
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = exposed_sexual
						has_character_flag = exposed_lover
					}
				}
				add_character_modifier = { name = known_sodomite years = 20 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_lover }
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = opinion_charge_deviant
					months = 24
				}
				spouse = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_angry
						years = 2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_religion }
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = opinion_accused_apostate
					months = 240
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_society }
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = opinion_charge_cultist
					months = 24
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_werewolf }
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = newly_found_werewolf
					months = 12
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_vampire }
				reverse_opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = newly_found_vampire
					months = 12
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = exposed_sexual
					has_character_flag = exposed_lover
				}
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = known_sodomite
					has_character_modifier = known_sodomite_pagan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3.0
				any_rival = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -20 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail rejected
letter_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.201
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.201
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Expose them
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.201
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
					has_character_flag = exposed_vampire
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = expoosed_sexual
							has_character_flag = exposed_lover
						}
						trait = homosexual
						NOT = { any_lover = { character = ROOT } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = exposed_werewolf } }
			
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
		
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_MYTH_WoL.9 }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = { 
					character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.6 } # Character uncovered as a werewolf
					save_event_target_as = target_discovered_werewolf
				}
				any_realm_character = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.7 } } # Court finds out character is a werewolf
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { FROM = { liege = { character = ROOT } } }
					}
					FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.8 } } } # Liege finds out character is a werewolf
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = exposed_vampire } }
			
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
			
			custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPA_VAMPIRE.17 }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.14 }# Character uncovered as a vampire
					save_event_target_as = target_discovered_vampire
				}
				any_realm_character = { character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.15 } } # Court finds out character is a vampire
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { FROM = { liege = { character = ROOT } } }
					}
					FROM = { liege = { character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.16 } } } # Liege finds out character is a vampire
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = exposed_sexual
						has_character_flag = exposed_lover
					}
					trait = homosexual
				}
			}
			
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.203 }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				clr_character_flag = exposed_sexual
				clr_character_flag = exposed_lover
				clr_character_flag = exposed_religion
				clr_character_flag = exposed_society
				clr_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
				clr_character_flag = exposed_vampire
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = monster_hunter
				FROM = { 
					NOR = {
						has_character_flag = exposed_sexual 
						has_character_flag = exposed_lover
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = zealous
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = gregarious
			}
		}
	}
	# Inform spouse
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.201
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_character_flag = exposed_lover
				NOT = { spouse = { character = ROOT } }
				any_lover = { NOT = {  character = ROOT } }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						trait = homosexual
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = known_sodomite
							has_character_modifier = known_sodomite_pagan
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:stalked = {
			spouse = {
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.202 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				clr_character_flag = exposed_sexual
				clr_character_flag = exposed_lover
				clr_character_flag = exposed_religion
				clr_character_flag = exposed_society
				clr_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
				clr_character_flag = exposed_vampire
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = shy
			}
		}
	}
	# Arrest them
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.201
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = exposed_religion
					has_character_flag = exposed_society
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			imprison = event_target:stalked
		}
		event_target:stalked = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.204 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = monster_hunter
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = reason_werewolf
					has_character_flag = reason_vampire
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 # Not the reason for the arrest, but you want to lock them up anyway
				trait = monster_hunter
				event_target:stalked = {
					is_monster_to_root = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
		}
	}
	# Do nothing
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.201
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				clr_character_flag = exposed_sexual
				clr_character_flag = exposed_lover
				clr_character_flag = exposed_religion
				clr_character_flag = exposed_society
				clr_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
				clr_character_flag = exposed_vampire
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = shy
			}
		}
	}
}

# Spouse informed of affair
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.202
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.202
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		event_target:stalked = {
			random_lover = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						character = FROM
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = target_adulterer
				if = {
					limit = { same_sex = PREV }
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_discovered_homosexual years = -1 }
					reverse_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_discovered_homosexual years = -1 }
				}
			}
			
		}
	}
	
	# Confront Spouse
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.202
		event_target:stalked = {
			character_event = { 
				id = 64001
				tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP64001"
			}
			character_event = { id = 20 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				any_lover = { character = event_target:stalked }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				event_target:stalked = {
					OR = {
						trait = lustful
						trait = seducer
						trait = seductress
						trait = hedonist
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Confront Lover
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.202
		event_target:stalked = {
			reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = committed_adultery_rumour years = 2 }
			character_event = { id = 20 }
		}
		event_target:target_adulterer = {
			character_event = { 
				id = 64002
				tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP64002"
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = envious
			}
		}
	}
	# Disbelieve
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.202
		opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_liar years = 1 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = paranoid
			}
		}
	}
	# Keep private
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.202
		opinion = { who = event_target:stalked modifier = opinion_unfaithful_private years = 2 }
		opinion = { who = event_target:target_adulterer modifier = opinion_cuckolded_private years = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = { trait = trusting }
			random = {
				chance = 30
				remove_trait = trusting
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = 38306 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}
		}
	}
}

# Homosexuality exposed
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.203
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.203
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.203
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = no }
			if = {
				limit = { religion_group = pagan_group }
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = known_sodomite_pagan
					years = 20
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = known_sodomite
					years = 20
				}
			}
			prestige = -500
			piety = -250
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }
			prestige = -100
			piety = -50
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clr_character_flag = exposed_sexual
			clr_character_flag = exposed_lover
			clr_character_flag = exposed_religion
			clr_character_flag = exposed_society
			clr_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
			clr_character_flag = exposed_vampire
		}
	}
}

# Imprisoned from findings
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.204
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	desc = {
		# Apostacy
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = exposed_religion
		}
		text = EVTDESCAMYTH_WoL.204
	}
	desc = {
		# Sedition
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = exposed_society
		}
		text = EVTDESCBMYTH_WoL.204
	}
	desc = {
		# Lycanthropy
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = exposed_werewolf
		}
		text = EVTDESCCMYTH_WoL.204
	}
	desc = {
		# Vampirism
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = exposed_vampire
		}
		text = EVTDESCDMYTH_WoL.204
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.204
		imprison = FROM
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = exposed_religion
					AND = {
						has_character_flag = exposed_society
						OR = {
							is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes
							is_secret_religious_society_member_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_accused_apostate 
				who = FROM
				years = 100
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes }
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = known_satanist
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = accused_apostate
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					religion = FROM
					controls_religion = no
					OR = {
						religion = catholic
						religion = fraticelli
						religion = orthodox
						religion = miaphysite
						religion = monophysite
						religion = monothelite
						religion = paulician
						religion = nestorian
						religion = yazidi
					}
				}
				add_trait = excommunicated
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_devil_worshiper_trigger = yes
							is_secret_religious_society_member_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					set_discovered_society = yes
					FROM = {
						save_event_target_as = my_liege
					}
					any_player = {
						limit = {
							primary_title = { always = yes }
							OR = {
								same_realm = ROOT
								is_close_relative = ROOT
								is_friend = ROOT
							}
							same_society_as = ROOT
							NOT = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
						character_event = { id = MNM.70400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = exposed_society
			}
			# Note - society might already have been partially handled above. If so, will already be listed as discovered
			change_society_currency = -200
			if = {
				limit = { is_society_grandmaster = yes }
				add_society_modifier = { modifier = grandmaster_exposed years = 10 }
			}
			else = {
				add_society_modifier = { modifier = member_exposed years = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_society_discovered_real = no }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_discovered_society = yes
					FROM = {
						save_event_target_as = my_liege
					}
					any_player = {
						limit = {
							primary_title = { always = yes }
							OR = {
								same_realm = ROOT
								is_close_relative = ROOT
								is_friend = ROOT
							}
							same_society_as = ROOT
							NOT = {
								character = ROOT
							}
						}
						character_event = { id = MNM.70400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_werewolf }
			opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
			add_trait = known_werewolf
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_character_modifier = known_monster
				remove_trait = secret_werewolf
			}
			any_realm_character = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.7 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = exposed_vampire }
			opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = exposed_me
			}
			add_trait = known_vampire
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_character_modifier = known_monster
				remove_trait = secret_vampire
			}
			any_realm_character = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
				character_event = { id = VAMPIRE.23 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Spouse demands you break up with lovers
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.205
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.205
	picture = GFX_evt_quarrel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Break up with lovers except spouses and concubines
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.205
		trigger = {
			any_lover = {
				NOT = { any_spouse = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { any_consort = { character = ROOT } }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = { modifier = opinion_unfaithful_private who = ROOT years = 2 }
		}
		any_lover = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { any_spouse = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { any_consort = { character = ROOT } }
			}
			remove_lover = ROOT
			character_event = { id = WoL.1005 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_WoL_1005 }
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.206 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = slut_seductress
				months = 24
			}
		}
		else = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_cuckolded_private
				months = 24
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				any_lover = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				any_friend = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				any_rival = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = chaste
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = arbitrary
			}
		}
	}
	# Break up with lovers except spouses but including concubines
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.205
		trigger = {
			any_lover = {
				NOT = { any_spouse = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { any_consort = { character = ROOT } }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = { modifier = opinion_angry who = ROOT years = 2 }
		}
		any_lover = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { any_spouse = { character = ROOT } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { any_consort = { character = ROOT } }
				opinion = { modifier = opinion_set_aside who = ROOT months = 1200 }
				remove_consort = ROOT
			}
			remove_lover = ROOT
			character_event = { id = WoL.1005 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_WoL_1005 }
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.206 } }
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = slut_seductress
				months = 24
			}
		}
		else = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_cuckolded_private
				months = 24
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				any_lover = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				any_friend = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				any_rival = { character = FROM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = chaste
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = arbitrary
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.205
		remove_lover = FROM
		remove_friend = FROM
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_lover = {
					NOT = { any_spouse = { character = ROOT } }
					NOT = { any_consort = { character = ROOT } }
				}
			}
			reverse_opinion = { modifier = opinion_unfaithful_private who = FROM years = 10 }
		}
		else = {
			reverse_opinion = { modifier = opinion_angry who = FROM years = 10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = slut_seductress
				months = 240
			}
		}
		else = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_cuckolded_private
				months = 240
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.207 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = lustful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					trait = seducer
					trait = seductress
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = hedonist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = proud
			}
		}
	}
}

# Herbalism - Work to cure Stressed/Depressed
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.213
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.213
	picture = GFX_evt_stressed_ruler
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
		OR = {
			trait = stressed
			trait = depressed
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Will select two ingredients, by prioritizing from the top, until it hits two available ones...
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_herb_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_animal_part_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_powder_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_liquid_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_herb_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_powder_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_animal_part_effect = yes
		select_random_hermetic_ingredient_liquid_effect = yes
	}
	
	# All effort
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.213
		random_list = {
			4 = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = TT_get_sick
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						random_list = {
							1 = {
								set_character_flag = got_pneumonia
							}
							3 = {
								set_character_flag = got_flu
							}
						}
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5000 days = 2 random = 4 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_trait = ill
				}
			}
			2 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					health = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					health = 7
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					health = 10
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					health = 15
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			random = {
				chance = 70
				remove_trait = stressed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }
			random = {
				chance = 70
				remove_trait = depressed
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				health = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				health = 7
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				health = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				health = 15
			}
		}
	}
	# Use easy to access ingredients
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.213
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			random = {
				chance = 30
				remove_trait = stressed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = depressed }
			random = {
				chance = 30
				remove_trait = depressed
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	# Use an ingredient on-hand
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.213
		trigger = {
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = ingredient
			}
		}
		tooltip_info = yes
		custom_tooltip = { text = tt_ingredient_available }
		if = {
			limit = { trait = stressed }
			random = {
				chance = 50
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.9
					has_selected_herb_ingredient_1_trigger = yes
				}
				remove_trait = stressed
			}
			if = {
				limit = { trait = depressed }
				random = {
					chance = 30
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.9
						has_selected_herb_ingredient_1_trigger = yes
					}
					remove_trait = depressed
				}
			}
		}
		destroy_selected_ingredient_1_effect = yes
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 3 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_selected_herb_ingredient_1_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	# Just accept your issues
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.213
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

			religion_authority = 0.3

			religion_authority = 0.6

# Intrigued by an ancient religion
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.215
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_norse }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_NORSE
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_tengri }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_TENGRI
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_baltic }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_BALTIC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_finnish }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_FINNISH
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_slavic }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_SLAVIC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_west_african }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_WEST_AFRICAN
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_zun }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_ZUN
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_draconic }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_DRACONIC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_celtic }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_CELTIC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_jotnar }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_JOTNAR
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_greek }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_GREEK
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_egyptian }
		text = EVTDESC_MYTH_WoL_215_EGYPTIAN
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_monk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Convert
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_MYTH_WoL.215
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag
			event_ancient_religion_norse		= { religion = norse_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_tengri		= { religion = tengri_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_baltic		= { religion = baltic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_finnish		= { religion = finnish_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_slavic		= { religion = slavic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_west_african	= { religion = west_african_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_zun			= { religion = zun_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_draconic		= { religion = draconic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_celtic		= { religion = druidic }
			event_ancient_religion_jotnar		= { religion = jotnar }
			event_ancient_religion_greek		= { religion = hellenic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_egyptian		= { religion = kemetic_pagan }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = honest
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Convert in secret
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_MYTH_WoL.215
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag
			event_ancient_religion_norse		= { set_secret_religion = norse_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_tengri		= { set_secret_religion = tengri_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_baltic		= { set_secret_religion = baltic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_finnish		= { set_secret_religion = finnish_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_slavic		= { set_secret_religion = slavic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_west_african	= { set_secret_religion = west_african_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_zun			= { set_secret_religion = zun_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_draconic		= { set_secret_religion = draconic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_celtic		= { set_secret_religion = druidic }
			event_ancient_religion_jotnar		= { set_secret_religion = jotnar }
			event_ancient_religion_greek		= { set_secret_religion = hellenic_pagan }
			event_ancient_religion_egyptian		= { set_secret_religion = kemetic_pagan }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = deceitful
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_MYTH_WoL.215
		add_trait = zealous
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = cynical } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 
				ai_zeal >= 50
			}
		}
	}
	
	# Disappointed
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD_MYTH_WoL.215
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = cynical } }
			add_trait = cynical
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 
				ai_zeal < 0
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_norse
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_tengri
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_baltic
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_finnish
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_slavic
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_west_african
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_zun
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_draconic
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_celtic
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_jotnar
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_greek
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_roman
		clr_character_flag = event_ancient_religion_egyptian
	}
}

# Search for herbs in the forest
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.216
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = apprentice_herb_gather } }
		text = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.216
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_character_flag = apprentice_herb_gather }
		text = EVTDESCBMYTH_WoL.216
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_experiment
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.216
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.217 days = 50 random = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.216
		trigger = { ai = no }
		remove_character_modifier = acquire_ingredients_decision_cooldown_timer
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.217
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			which = gath_try
			value = 5
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = gath_res
			value = 0
		}
		
		export_to_variable = { which = search_skill value = stewardship }
		export_to_variable = { which = temp value = learning }
		change_variable = { which = search_skill which = temp }
		set_variable = { which = temp value = 0 }
		
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gath_try
					value = 1
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { # Successful gathering
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = search_skill value = 10 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.6
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = search_skill value = 14 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.7
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = search_skill value = 18 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = search_skill value = 24 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = search_skill value = 28 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.2
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = search_skill value = 32 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.1
						trait = herbalist
					}
					
					change_variable = {
						which = gath_res
						value = 1
					}
				}
				50 = { # Unsuccessful gathering
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						trait = drunkard
					}
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = gath_try
				value = 1
			}
		}
		
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.218 }
	}
}

	id = MYTH_WoL.218

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gath_res
					value = 4
				}
			}
			check_variable = {
				which = gath_res
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESCCMYTH_WoL.218
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gath_res
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.218
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = gath_res
				value = 4
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIP_MNM_1812 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.218
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gath_res
					value = 4
				}
			}
			check_variable = {
				which = gath_res
				value = 1
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIP_MNM_1812 }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.218
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gath_res
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			120 = { #no effect
				
			}
			60 = { #poisoned
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
					give_food_poisoning_effect = yes
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = EVTTOOLTIP_MNM_1812_ILL
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" } }
					add_trait = ill
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = apprentice_herb_gather }
			subtract_variable = { which = gath_res value = 1 }
			liege = { hermetic_add_herbal_ingredient_effect = yes }
			clr_character_flag = apprentice_herb_gather
			liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 random = 2 } }
		}
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 }
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gath_res
					value = 1
				}
			}
			hermetic_add_herbal_ingredient_effect = yes
			
			subtract_variable = {
				which = gath_res
				value = 1
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = do_not_disturb
	}
}

				trigger = { has_character_modifier = black_eye }

					set_character_flag = healed_black_eye

					set_character_flag = healed_swollen_ankle
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = { has_character_modifier = concussion }

					set_character_flag = healed_concussion
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = { has_character_modifier = cracked_ribs }
				remove_character_modifier = cracked_ribs
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = healed_cracked_ribs
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = { has_character_modifier = badly_bruised }
				remove_character_modifier = badly_bruised
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = healed_badly_bruised
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.220 } }
		}
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = healed_wounded
			clr_character_flag = healed_maimed
			clr_character_flag = healed_scarred
			clr_character_flag = healed_disfigured
			clr_character_flag = healed_one_eyed
			clr_character_flag = healed_one_handed
			clr_character_flag = healed_one_legged
			clr_character_flag = healed_mangled
			clr_character_flag = healed_eunuch
			clr_character_flag = healed_blinded
			clr_character_flag = healed_severely_injured
			clr_character_flag = healed_black_eye
			clr_character_flag = healed_swollen_wrist
			clr_character_flag = healed_swollen_ankle
			clr_character_flag = healed_concussion
			clr_character_flag = healed_cracked_ribs
			clr_character_flag = healed_badly_bruised
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {

			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = maimed
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = disfigured
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = one_eyed
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = one_handed
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = one_legged
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = mangled
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = eunuch
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = blinded
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = REFUSE_POTION
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				trait = paranoid
				has_potion_modifer_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { character = FROM }
			custom_tooltip = { text = tt_no_refund }
		}
		else = {
