		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				character = FROM
			}

				factor = 2

			}

		name = EXCELLENT
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = healed_wounded } }
			tooltip = { remove_trait = wounded }
			clr_character_flag = healed_wounded
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = healed_maimed } }

					}

				trigger = { trait = gluttonous }

			}
		}
		if = {

				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = regeneration_strain
					has_character_modifier = potion_of_battle

					has_character_modifier = potion_of_health

			}
		}

			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = REFUSE_POTION
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no

				has_potion_modifer_trigger = yes
			}

	}

			chance = 20

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = minor_disease_herpes }
				remove_character_modifier = minor_disease_herpes
			}
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.228 } }

					has_character_modifier = potion_of_purity
					has_character_modifier = potion_of_battle
					has_character_modifier = potion_of_health
					has_character_modifier = potion_of_secrets

				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {

				NOT = { num_of_children = 1 }

		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = REFUSE_POTION

			OR = {
				ai = no
				trait = paranoid
				has_potion_modifer_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { character = FROM }
			custom_tooltip = { text = tt_no_refund }
		}
		else = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.234 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				character = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_character_modifier = regeneration_strain
			}

# Potion poisoning - can occur if you take a potion with a linger effect while one is already present
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.232
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.232
	picture = GFX_evt_illness
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.232
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = Reapers }
			add_trait = food_poisoning
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = ill
		}
		set_character_flag = manifest_food_poisoning
		scrying_omen_fulfilled_by_gaining_disease_effect = yes
		father = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no 
					is_liege_of = ROOT
				}
				set_character_flag = announce_food_poisoning
				character_event = { id = RIP.5060 }
			}
		}
		mother = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					ai = no 
					is_liege_of = ROOT
				}
				set_character_flag = announce_food_poisoning
				character_event = { id = RIP.5060 }
			}
		}
		spouse = {
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				set_character_flag = announce_food_poisoning
				character_event = { id = RIP.5060 }
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.233 days = 30 random = 15 }
	}
}

	id = MYTH_WoL.233
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.233

		remove_trait = food_poisoning
		remove_trait = ill
		remove_character_modifier = potion_of_purity
		remove_character_modifier = potion_of_battle
		remove_character_modifier = potion_of_fertility
		remove_character_modifier = potion_of_health
		remove_character_modifier = potion_of_secrets
	}
}

# Make an experimental potion from spare ingredients
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.235
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.235
	picture = GFX_evt_experiment
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		OR = {
			trait = herbalist
			has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
		}
		ROOT = {
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = ingredient
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_1
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_2
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_3
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_4
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_5
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_6
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_7
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_8
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_9
			has_character_modifier = experimental_potion_10
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		select_random_magic_ingredient_effect = yes
		select_random_magic_ingredient_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.235
		trigger = {
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			9 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_1 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_animal_part_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_2 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_metal_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_3 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 2
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_4 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 3
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_5 months = 6 }
				}
				else = {
					# Fallback to herb potion
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_1 months = 6 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_6 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_animal_part_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_7 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_metal_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_8 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 2
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_9 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_1
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 3
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_10 months = 6 }
				}
				else = {
					# Fallback to herb potion
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_6 months = 6 }
				}
			}
		}
		destroy_selected_ingredient_1_effect = yes
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 2 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.235
		trigger = {
			any_artifact = {
				has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			9 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_1 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_animal_part_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_2 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_metal_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_3 months = 6 }

							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 3

					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_5 months = 6 }
				}
				else = {
					# Fallback to herb potion
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_1 months = 6 }
				}
			}
			1 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_6 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_animal_part_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_7 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_metal_trigger = yes
							quality == 1
						}
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_8 months = 6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_artifact = {
							has_artifact_flag = selected_ingredient_2
							is_ingredient_herb_trigger = yes
							quality == 2
						}
					}

# Weird Scholarship Necromancy event
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.236
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.236
	picture = GFX_evt_book_carolingian_script
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_scholarship
		has_education_magic_trigger = yes
		prisoner = no
		is_incapable = no
		any_artifact = { artifact_type = necronomicon }
		NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
		has_character_modifier = weird_scholar
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			trait = eldritch_scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = veteran_wizard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = arcane_master
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.236
		piety = -100
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.137 days = 10 random = 50 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				religion = satanist
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.236
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.236
		piety = 200
		destroy_artifact = necronomicon
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = zealous
			}
		}
	}
}

			set_undead_culture = yes

		add_trait = necromancer
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_necromancy_study = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.238
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				lifestyle_traits = 1
			}
		}
		event_target:new_undead = {} # For icon
	}
}

			dynasty = none
		}
		new_character = {
			set_undead_culture = yes
			religion = the_damned
			save_event_target_as = new_undead
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.239
		event_target:new_undead = {} # For icon
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.237 days = 10 random = 40 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = diligent
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.239
		event_target:new_undead = {} # For icon
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_theology
		has_education_magic_trigger = yes
		prisoner = no
		is_incapable = no
		NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				# Demon demands gold
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.244 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Demon demands life of heir
				trigger = {
					current_heir = { is_child_of = ROOT }
				}
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.245 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Terrible demon marriage
				trigger = {	is_married = no }
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.246 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Demon demands regular sacrifices
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.247 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Pestilence demon
				trigger = { has_dlc = Reapers }
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.248 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Lustful demon
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.249 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Gluttonous demon
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.250 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Wrathful demon
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.251 }
			}
			1 = {
				# Greedy demon
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.252 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Demon demands fulfillment of a marriage contract
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.246
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.246
	picture = GFX_evt_uncomfortable
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = no }
			create_character = {
				age = 26
				dynasty = random
				attributes = {
					martial = 0
					diplomacy = 0
					stewardship = 0
					intrigue = 0
					learning = 3
				}
				health = 6.0
				fertility = 0.8
				female = yes
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = summoner
				trait = clubfooted
				trait = harelip
				trait = hunchback
				trait = lisp
				trait = stutter
				trait = ugly
				trait = weak
				trait = gluttonous
				trait = envious
				trait = humble
				trait = shy
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_character = {
				age = 26
				dynasty = random
				attributes = {
					martial = 0
					diplomacy = 0
					stewardship = 0
					intrigue = 0
					learning = 3
				}
				health = 6.0
				fertility = 0.8
				female = no
				religion = ROOT
				culture = ROOT
				trait = novice_mage
				trait = summoner
				trait = clubfooted
				trait = harelip
				trait = hunchback
				trait = lisp
				trait = stutter
				trait = ugly
				trait = weak
				trait = gluttonous
				trait = envious
				trait = humble
				trait = shy
				trait = trusting
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = vampire }
			new_character = { add_trait = vampire }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { trait = werewolf }
			new_character = { add_trait = werewolf }
		}
		new_character = { save_event_target_as = new_spouse }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.246
		add_trait = necromancer
		event_target:new_spouse = {}
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = no }
			add_spouse = event_target:new_spouse
		}
		else = {
			add_spouse_matrilineal = event_target:new_spouse
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_necromancy_study = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.246
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:new_spouse = { 
				death = {
					death_reason = death_missing
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Lust demon
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.249
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.249
	picture = GFX_evt_shady_meeting
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				spouse = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_female = yes
							NOT = { trait = homosexual }
						}
						AND = {
							is_female = no
							trait = homosexual
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				age = 357
				attributes = {
					martial = 3
					diplomacy = 7
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 10
					learning = 4
				}
				health = 6
				female = no
				religion = satanist
				culture = demon_culture
				dynasty = random
				trait = demon_trait
				trait = seducer
				trait = lustful
				trait = gregarious
			}
			new_character = {
				set_focus = focus_seduction
				set_character_flag = cant_ask_to_leave
				save_event_target_as = new_demon
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_character = {
				age = 357
				attributes = {
					martial = 3
					diplomacy = 7
					stewardship = 5
					intrigue = 10
					learning = 4
				}
				health = 6
				female = yes
				religion = satanist
				culture = demon_culture
				dynasty = random
				trait = demon_trait
				trait = seductress
				trait = lustful
				trait = gregarious
				immortal_age = 33
			}
			new_character = {
				set_focus = focus_seduction
				save_event_target_as = new_demon
				set_character_flag = cant_ask_to_leave
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				spouse = { trait = homosexual }
			}
			event_target:new_demon = { add_trait = homosexual }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.249
		add_trait = necromancer
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:new_demon = {
				ROOT = {
					spouse = {
						event_target:new_demon = {
							opinion = {
								who = PREV
								modifier = opinion_seducing
								years = 1000
							}
							character_event = { id = WoL.100 days = 1 } # No warning - Let the chase begin!
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.253 years = 10 }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_necromancy_study = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					num_of_spouses = 2
					num_of_consorts = 1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = envious
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.249
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:new_demon = { 
				death = {
					death_reason = death_missing
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Gluttony demon wipes prosperity
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.254
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				set_variable = { which = prosperity_value value = 0 }
				random = {
				chance = 85 #chance to lower by 1 step
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = prosperity_modifier_1
						}
						remove_province_modifier = prosperity_modifier_1
						break = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = prosperity_modifier_2
						}
						remove_province_modifier = prosperity_modifier_2
						add_province_modifier = { name = prosperity_modifier_1 duration = -1 }
						break = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = prosperity_modifier_3
						}
						remove_province_modifier = prosperity_modifier_3
						add_province_modifier = { name = prosperity_modifier_2 duration = -1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		repeat_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.254 days = 365 }
	}
}

# Greed demon steals money
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.256
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			export_to_variable = { which = my_wealth value = wealth }
			divide_variable = { which = my_wealth value = 10 }
			multiply_variable = { which = my_wealth value = -1 }
			wealth = my_wealth
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = { which = my_wealth which = PREV }
				multiply_variable = { which = my_wealth value = -1 }
				wealth = my_wealth
			}
		}
		export_to_variable = { which = my_wealth value = wealth }
		divide_variable = { which = my_wealth value = 10 }
		multiply_variable = { which = my_wealth value = -1 }
		wealth = my_wealth

	}

# Magic or Scholarship + Necromancer councillor
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.261
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_focus = focus_magic
			has_focus = focus_scholarship
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = had_necromancer_friend_event }
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy }
		has_education_magic_trigger = yes
		is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
		OR = {
			job_spiritual = {
				AND = {
					trait = necromancer
					prisoner = no
					is_incapable = no
					is_inaccessible_trigger = no
					personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
				}
			}
			job_marshal = {
				AND = {
					trait = necromancer
					prisoner = no
					is_incapable = no
					is_inaccessible_trigger = no
					personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
				}
			}

				AND = {
					trait = necromancer
					prisoner = no
					is_incapable = no
					is_inaccessible_trigger = no
					personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
				}
			}

					trait = necromancer
					prisoner = no
					is_incapable = no
					is_inaccessible_trigger = no

				}

					reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }

					prisoner = no

					reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = stressed
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = depressed
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Determine which character to use
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					has_minor_title = title_court_physician
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					prisoner = no
					is_incapable = no
					is_inaccessible_trigger = no

				}

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

					AND = {
						trait = necromancer
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						is_inaccessible_trigger = no
						personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
						reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					}
				}
			}
			# Ping to set FROM
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.262 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				job_marshal = {
					AND = {
						trait = necromancer
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						is_inaccessible_trigger = no
						personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
						reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					}
				}
			}
			# Ping to set FROM
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.262 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				job_chancellor = {
					AND = {
						trait = necromancer
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						is_inaccessible_trigger = no
						personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
						reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					}
				}
			}
			# Ping to set FROM
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.262 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				job_treasurer = {
					AND = {
						trait = necromancer
						prisoner = no
						is_incapable = no
						is_inaccessible_trigger = no
						personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
						reverse_personal_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 75 }
					}
				}
			}
			# Ping to set FROM
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.262 }
		}

# 273 - Completed resurrection. Can gain Necromancer
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.273
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.273
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			culture = FROMFROMFROM
			religion = FROMFROMFROM
			dynasty = none
		}
		new_character = {
			set_undead_culture = yes
			religion = the_damned
			opinion = { modifier = opinion_controlled_undead who = ROOT years = 700 }
			opinion = { modifier = opinion_controlled_undead who = FROMFROMFROM years = 700 }
			save_event_target_as = new_undead
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.273
		add_trait = necromancer
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_friend = FROMFROMFROM } }
			add_friend = FROMFROMFROM
		}
		event_target:new_undead = {}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_necromancy_study = yes
			FROMFROMFROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.276 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.273
		event_target:new_undead = {}
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
	after = {
		FROMFROMFROM = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.273 } }
	}
}

# Automatically set field of magic study
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.277
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		NOR = {
			has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
			has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
			has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
			has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
			has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		}
		OR = {
			trait = summoner
			trait = enchanter
			trait = alchemist
			trait = herbalist
			trait = necromancer
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = summoner
					AND = {
						has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
						liege = { trait = summoner }
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = studying_conjuration duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = enchanter
					AND = {
						has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
						liege = { trait = enchanter }
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = studying_sorcery duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = alchemist
					AND = {
						has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
						liege = { trait = alchemist }
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = studying_alchemy duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = herbalist
					AND = {
						has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
						liege = { trait = herbalist }
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = studying_herbalism duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = necromancer
					AND = {
						has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
						liege = { trait = necromancer }
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = { name = studying_necromancy duration = -1 }
		}
	}
}

# Necromancer - Perform divination

	id = MYTH_WoL.278

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_capable = yes
	has_dlc = Mystics
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		NOR = {
			has_character_modifier = good_battle_omen
			has_character_modifier = bad_battle_omen
			has_character_modifier = good_relationship_omen
			has_character_modifier = bad_relationship_omen
			has_character_modifier = good_power_omen
			has_character_modifier = bad_power_omen
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.278
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = good_battle_omen duration = -1 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = bad_battle_omen duration = -1 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = good_relationship_omen duration = -1 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = bad_relationship_omen duration = -1 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = good_power_omen duration = -1 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = bad_power_omen duration = -1 } }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.278
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

		has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		any_rival = {
			higher_tier_than = BARON
			NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.279
		custom_tooltip = { text = tt_disease_rival }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_rival = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = BARON
					NOT = { vassal_of = ROOT }
				}
				capital_scope = {
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							spawn_disease = tuberculosis
						}
						1 = {
							spawn_disease = typhoid_fever
						}
						1 = {
							spawn_disease = typhus
						}
						1 = {
							spawn_disease = measles
						}
						1 = {
							spawn_disease = small_pox
						}
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.279
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_intrigue }
				add_character_modifier = { name = intrigue_drained years = 3 }
				ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = drained_intrigue years = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_learning }
				add_character_modifier = { name = learning_drained years = 3 }

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			additive_opinion_modifier = {
				factor = -0.28
				who = event_target:character_1
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:character_2 value = 0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				opinion = { who = event_target:character_2 value = 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				opinion = { who = event_target:character_2 value = 75 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.280
		trigger = { event_target:character_3 = { always = yes } }
		event_target:character_3 = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_diplo }
				add_character_modifier = { name = diplomacy_drained years = 3 }
				ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = drained_diplomacy years = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_martial }
				add_character_modifier = { name = martial_drained years = 3 }
				ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = drained_martial years = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_stewardship }
				add_character_modifier = { name = stewardship_drained years = 3 }
				ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = drained_stewardship years = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_intrigue }
				add_character_modifier = { name = intrigue_drained years = 3 }
				ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = drained_intrigue years = 3 } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = drain_learning }
				add_character_modifier = { name = learning_drained years = 3 }
				ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = drained_learning years = 3 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			additive_opinion_modifier = {
				factor = -0.28
				who = event_target:character_3
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:character_1 value = 0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				opinion = { who = event_target:character_3 value = 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				opinion = { who = event_target:character_3 value = 75 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.280
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			event_target:character_1 = {
				clr_character_flag = drain_diplo
				clr_character_flag = drain_martial
				clr_character_flag = drain_stewardship
				clr_character_flag = drain_intrigue
				clr_character_flag = drain_learning
			}
			event_target:character_2 = {
				clr_character_flag = drain_diplo
				clr_character_flag = drain_martial
				clr_character_flag = drain_stewardship
				clr_character_flag = drain_intrigue
				clr_character_flag = drain_learning
			}
			event_target:character_3 = {
				clr_character_flag = drain_diplo
				clr_character_flag = drain_martial
				clr_character_flag = drain_stewardship
				clr_character_flag = drain_intrigue
				clr_character_flag = drain_learning
			}
		}
	}

						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_tuberculosis }

						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_typhus }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_bubonic_plague }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_measles }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_smallpox }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_syphilis }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_flu }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_aztec_disease }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_dysentery }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_pneumonia }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_rabies }
						1 = { set_character_flag = immune_zombie_plague }
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {

		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 random = 3 }
	}

		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.281
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

# Recent deaths are an opportunity
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.282
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.282
	picture = GFX_evt_bring_out_your_dead
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_capable = yes
	has_dlc = Reapers
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
		any_demesne_province = { has_province_modifier = depopulated_3 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.282
		scaled_wealth = -0.3
		piety = -20
		any_demesne_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = depopulated_3 }
			owner = {
				spawn_unit = {
					province = PREV
					home = ROOT
					owner = ROOT
					leader = none
					troops = {
						zombie_troops = { 100 100 }
					}
					match_character = ROOT
					match_mult = 0.05
					match_min = 100
					match_max = 500
					cannot_inherit = yes
					attrition = 0.2
					maintenance_multiplier = 0.2
					can_toggle_looting = no
					reinforces = no
					earmark = event_zombie
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_disease = yes
					ROOT = {
						immune_to_infection = no
					}
					random = 40
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						disease = tuberculosis
						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_tuberculosis
								has_character_flag = got_tuberculosis
								trait = has_tuberculosis
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						clr_character_flag = disease_not_serious
						set_character_flag = got_tuberculosis
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5015 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						disease = typhoid_fever
						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_typhoid_fever
								has_character_flag = got_typhoid_fever
								trait = has_typhoid_fever
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						clr_character_flag = disease_not_serious
						set_character_flag = got_typhoid_fever
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5016 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						disease = typhus
						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_typhus
								has_character_flag = got_typhus
								trait = has_typhus
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						clr_character_flag = disease_not_serious
						set_character_flag = got_typhus
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5017 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						disease = bubonic_plague
						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_bubonic_plague
								has_character_flag = got_bubonic_plague
								trait = has_bubonic_plague
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						clr_character_flag = disease_not_serious
						set_character_flag = got_bubonic_plague
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5012 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						disease = bubonic_plague
						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_bubonic_plague
								has_character_flag = got_bubonic_plague
								trait = has_bubonic_plague
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						clr_character_flag = disease_not_serious
						set_character_flag = got_bubonic_plague
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5012 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {

						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_measles
								has_character_flag = got_measles

							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						clr_character_flag = disease_not_serious
						set_character_flag = got_measles
						set_character_flag = developing_illness
						character_event = { id = RIP.5018 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						disease = small_pox
						ROOT = {
							NOR = {
								has_character_flag = immune_smallpox

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.284
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.284
	picture = GFX_evt_experiment
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	show_from_from = yes
	
	ai = no
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.284
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { trait = enchanter }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
						has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
						has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
						has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
					}
				}
				remove_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
				remove_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
				remove_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
				remove_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_1
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery } }
				add_character_modifier = { modifier = studying_sorcery duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { trait = summoner }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
						has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
						has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
						has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
					}
				}
				remove_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
				remove_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
				remove_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
				remove_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_1
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration } }
				add_character_modifier = { modifier = studying_conjuration duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
						has_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
						has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
						has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
					}
				}
				remove_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
				remove_character_modifier = studying_herbalism
				remove_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
				remove_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_1
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy } }
				add_character_modifier = { modifier = studying_alchemy duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { trait = herbalist }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
						has_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
						has_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
						has_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
					}
				}
				remove_character_modifier = studying_sorcery
				remove_character_modifier = studying_alchemy
				remove_character_modifier = studying_conjuration
				remove_character_modifier = studying_necromancy
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_1
				remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2

			}
		}
		else_if = {

# Further apprenticeship. After 9 years, get a lifestyle
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.285
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
		NOT = { lifestyle_traits = 1 }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		change_variable = { which = apprentice_years value = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = apprentice_years value = 9 } }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.286 }
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.286
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.286
	picture = GFX_evt_experiment
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.286
		remove_character_modifier = magic_study_1
		remove_character_modifier = magic_study_2
		set_variable = { which = apprentice_years value = 0 }
		change_learning = 1
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = enchanter } }
			add_trait = enchanter
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = summoner } }
			add_trait = summoner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = alchemist } }
			add_trait = alchemist
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = herbalist } }
			add_trait = herbalist
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = necromancer } }
			add_trait = necromancer
		}
		liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.287 } }
	}
}

			limit = { trait = summoner }
			tooltip = { FROM = { add_trait = summoner } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = alchemist }
			tooltip = { FROM = { add_trait = alchemist } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = herbalist }
			tooltip = { FROM = { add_trait = herbalist } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { trait = necromancer }

		FROM = { change_learning = 1 }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.290
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.290
	picture = GFX_evt_experiment
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_assigned_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
		NOT = { trait = stressed }
		NOT = {
			any_courtier_or_vassal = {
				has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
				has_character_modifier = magic_study_2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.290
		random = {
			chance = 25
			add_trait = stressed
		}
		any_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = { has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice }
			tooltip = {
				change_learning = 1
				if = {
					limit = { has_character_modifier = magic_study_1 }
					add_character_modifier = { modifier = magic_study_2 duration = -1 }
				}
				else = {
					add_character_modifier = { modifier = magic_study_1 duration = -1 }
				}
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.291 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.290
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.292
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.292
	picture = GFX_evt_recieve_letter
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_assigned_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
		any_courtier_or_vassal = {
			has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
			is_inaccessible_trigger = no
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		export_to_variable = { which = service_value value = scaled_wealth }
		divide_variable = { which = service_value value = 12 }
		any_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = { has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice }
			save_event_target_as = my_apprentice
		}
	}
	
	# Perform services
	option = {
		name = {
			trigger = { trait = enchanter }
			text = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.292
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { trait = summoner }
			text = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.292
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { trait = herbalist }
			text = EVTOPTCMYTH_WoL.292
		}
		name = {
			trigger = { trait = alchemist }
			text = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.292
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = necromancer } }
		wealth = service_value
		event_target:my_apprentice = {
			set_variable = { which = service_value which = ROOT }
			divide_variable = { which = service_value value = 2 }
			tooltip = { wealth = service_value }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.293 }
		}
	}
	
	# Clean and prepare ritual area
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEMYTH_WoL.292
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = alchemist
				trait = herbalist
			}
		}
		piety = 20
		event_target:my_apprentice = {
			tooltip = { piety =  10 }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.294 }
		}
	}
	
	# Gather ingredients
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFMYTH_WoL.292
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = alchemist
				trait = herbalist
			}
		}
		event_target:my_apprentice = {
			set_character_flag = apprentice_herb_gather
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.216 }
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 75 }
		}
	}
	
	# Mystic cleansing
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTGMYTH_WoL.292
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = alchemist
				trait = herbalist
			}
			OR = {
				has_character_modifier = cursed
				has_character_modifier = haunted_castle
				has_character_modifier = diplomacy_drained
				has_character_modifier = martial_drained
				has_character_modifier = stewardship_drained
				has_character_modifier = intrigue_drained
				has_character_modifier = learning_drained
				has_character_modifier = voice_of_satan
				has_character_modifier = mystic_treatment_poor
				has_character_modifier = mystic_treatment_terrible
				has_character_modifier = cant_stop_dancing
				has_character_modifier = phantom_pain
				has_character_modifier = frightening_visions
				has_character_modifier = withdrawal_symptoms
				has_character_modifier = corrupting_magic_minor
				has_character_modifier = corrupting_magic_major
				capital_scope = {
					OR = { 
						has_province_modifier = night_spirits
						has_province_modifier = local_death_cult
					}
				}
			}
		}
		tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = cursed }
					remove_character_modifier = cursed
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = haunted_castle }
					remove_character_modifier = haunted_castle
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = diplomacy_drained }
					remove_character_modifier = diplomacy_drained
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = martial_drained }
					remove_character_modifier = martial_drained
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = stewardship_drained }
					remove_character_modifier = stewardship_drained
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = intrigue_drained }
					remove_character_modifier = intrigue_drained
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = learning_drained }
					remove_character_modifier = learning_drained
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = voice_of_satan }
					remove_character_modifier = voice_of_satan
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = mystic_treatment_poor }
					remove_character_modifier = mystic_treatment_poor
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = mystic_treatment_terrible }
					remove_character_modifier = mystic_treatment_terrible
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = cant_stop_dancing }
					remove_character_modifier = cant_stop_dancing
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = phantom_pain }
					remove_character_modifier = phantom_pain
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = frightening_visions }
					remove_character_modifier = frightening_visions
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = withdrawal_symptoms }
					remove_character_modifier = withdrawal_symptoms
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = corrupting_magic_minor }
					remove_character_modifier = corrupting_magic_minor
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = corrupting_magic_major }
					remove_character_modifier = corrupting_magic_major
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { capital_scope = { has_province_modifier = night_spirits } }
					capital_scope = { remove_province_modifier = night_spirits }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { capital_scope = { has_province_modifier = local_death_cult } }
					capital_scope = { remove_province_modifier = local_death_cult }
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:my_apprentice = {
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.295 }
		}
	}
	# Read and organize notes
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTHMYTH_WoL.292
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				trait = herbalist
				trait = alchemist
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = { modifier = organized_notes years = 1 }
		event_target:my_apprentice = {
			tooltip = {
				add_character_modifier = { modifier = organized_notes years = 1 }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.296 }
		}
	}
	# Do nothing
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTIMYTH_WoL.292
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
	
	after = {
		set_variable = { which = service_value value = 0 }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.293
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.293
	picture = GFX_evt_market
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.293
		wealth = service_value
		set_variable = { which = service_value value = 0 }
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 random = 2 }
		liege = { character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 1 random = 2 } }
	}
}

	id = MYTH_WoL.295

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {

		liege = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_character_modifier = cursed }

# Experimental potions
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.297
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.297
	picture = GFX_evt_experiment
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_focus = focus_magic
		has_minor_title = title_mage_apprentice
		liege = { trait = herbalist }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAMYTH_WoL.297
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_1 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_2 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_3 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_4 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_5 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_6 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_7 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_8 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_9 months = 12 } }
				1 = { add_character_modifier = { name = experimental_potion_10 months = 12 } }
			}
			character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.40 days = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTBMYTH_WoL.297
		trigger = { ai = no }
	}
}

# MYTH_WoL.298 - Choose magic specialization, page 2
character_event = {
	id = MYTH_WoL.298
	title = EVTNAMEMYTH_WoL.39
	desc = EVTDESCMYTH_WoL.39
	picture = GFX_evt_comet
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Study herbalism - does not require magic
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTDMYTH_WoL.39
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = { name = studying_herbalism duration = -1 }
	}
	
	# Necromancy
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTFMYTH_WoL.39
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					trait = novice_mage
					trait = eldritch_scholar
					trait = veteran_wizard
					trait = arcane_master
				}
				any_owned_bloodline = {
					has_bloodline_flag = allow_necromancy_study
				}
			}
		}
		prestige = 5
		add_character_modifier = { name = studying_necromancy duration = -1 }
	}
	
	# Back to the first page
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTEMYTH_WoL.39
		character_event = { id = MYTH_WoL.39 }
	}
}
